# Implementation Journal — Part 1

> Phases 1–133: Full compiler implementation from HIR foundation through conformance hardening. Highlights: E2E tests, benchmark suite, Babel differential analysis, headless render comparison, P0 critical bug fixes, conformance rate 13.4% → 23.5% (403/1717). Recent: expected file rebaseline with compilationMode:"all" (+9 net, +88 newly passing, 79 reclassified), validation fixes, mutation range propagation fixes (+93 fixtures).

---

## Phase 180: Extend IdVec/IdSet Adoption to 4 Validation Passes (0 conformance change)

**Date:** 2026-04-05
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Group J1: Replace HashMap<IdentifierId, T> with indexed Vec<T>
**Upstream:** N/A (Rust-specific optimization, no upstream equivalent)

Extended the IdVec/IdSet adoption from Phase 179 to 4 additional validation passes. Each file had multiple FxHashMap<IdentifierId, T> and FxHashSet<IdentifierId> patterns converted to O(1) indexed collections. Key patterns: `.get(&id)` becomes `.get(id)`, `.contains(&id)` becomes `.contains(id)`, `.entry(id).or_insert(...)` becomes `entry_or_insert_with(id, ...)` or `contains_key`/`insert`, `FxHashSet::default()` becomes `IdSet::new()`, `.iter()/.into_iter()` on sets becomes `.iter_indices()` with `IdentifierId(idx as u32)` reconstruction. The `FxHashMap<String, T>` and `FxHashSet<&str>` patterns (string-keyed, not ID-keyed) were left unchanged.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_hooks_usage.rs` | Converted id_to_name, hook_callee_ids, is_stable_hook_by_id, conditional_blocks to IdVec/IdSet |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` | Converted id_to_name, hook_return_ids, func_captures, func_bodies, iife_ids, fn_expr_ids, effect_callback_ids, ref_ids, ref_hook_result_ids, local_id_map to IdVec/IdSet |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_ref_access_in_render.rs` | Converted ref_ids, non_render_ids, id_to_name, id_aliases, fe_bodies, local_ref_ids to IdVec/IdSet |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_global_reassignment.rs` | Converted id_to_name, safe_ids, id_aliases, id_to_assigned_name, undeclared_load_ids, global_load_ids to IdVec/IdSet |

## Phase 179: Add IdVec/IdSet Types and Initial Pass Conversions (0 conformance change)

**Date:** 2026-04-05
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Group J1: Replace HashMap<IdentifierId, T> with indexed Vec<T>
**Upstream:** N/A (Rust-specific optimization, no upstream equivalent)

Added `IdVec<Id, T>` and `IdSet<Id>` indexed collection types to `types.rs` as O(1) replacements for `FxHashMap<IdentifierId, T>` and `FxHashSet<IdentifierId>`. Since `IdentifierId` is a sequential `u32`, `Vec`-backed collections provide better cache locality and no hashing overhead compared to hash maps/sets.

Converted 6 passes as initial adoption: `validate_no_eval`, `validate_no_capitalized_calls`, `validate_no_set_state_in_effects`, `rewrite_instruction_kinds`, `constant_propagation`, and `prune_temporary_lvalues`. The remaining 30+ files with `FxHashMap<IdentifierId, ...>` or `FxHashSet<IdentifierId>` patterns are left for incremental follow-up -- bulk automated conversion proved difficult due to the need to distinguish which `.get(&id)` and `.contains(&id)` calls are on IdVec/IdSet vs still-FxHashMap variables in the same file.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/types.rs` | Added `IdIndex` trait, `IdVec<Id, T>`, `IdSet<Id>` with full API |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_eval.rs` | FxHashSet -> IdSet |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_capitalized_calls.rs` | FxHashMap -> IdVec |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_set_state_in_effects.rs` | FxHashMap -> IdVec, FxHashSet -> IdSet |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/rewrite_instruction_kinds.rs` | FxHashMap -> IdVec, FxHashSet -> IdSet |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/optimization/constant_propagation.rs` | FxHashMap -> IdVec, FxHashSet -> IdSet |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/optimization/prune_temporary_lvalues.rs` | FxHashMap -> IdVec |

## Phase 178: Performance Optimization of Mutation/Aliasing Passes (0 conformance change, 21-35% speedup on large fixtures)

**Date:** 2026-04-05
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Group I: O(n^2+) Performance Regression in Mutation/Aliasing Passes
**Upstream:** `src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts`, `src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingRanges.ts`

Targeted performance optimizations for Pass 16 (`infer_mutation_aliasing_effects`) and Pass 20 (`infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges`), the two hottest passes in the pipeline. Measured via A/B benchmarking with the NAPI binary against the full benchmark suite.

**Pass 16 optimizations:**
- Sorted block processing: queued blocks are now sorted by block index before processing each iteration, improving forward-dataflow convergence speed. Previously blocks were processed in arbitrary HashMap drain order.
- Reused successor buffer: `terminal_successors` replaced with `terminal_successors_into` that pushes into a pre-allocated `Vec<BlockId>` instead of allocating a new Vec per block per iteration.
- Lightweight phi processing: `infer_phi_lightweight` takes pre-extracted `(IdentifierId, Vec<IdentifierId>)` instead of cloning full `Phi` structs (which contain `Place` with `Option<String>` and `Option<Box<ReactiveScope>>`).
- In-place state merging: `InferenceState::merge` now merges `AbstractValue` kinds and reasons in-place instead of allocating a new `AbstractValue` per merge via `merge_abstract_values`. The `reasons` FxHashSet is extended in-place rather than cloned.
- Reused sorted queue buffer across fixpoint iterations.

**Pass 20 optimizations:**
- Reusable BFS buffers: `BfsBuffers` struct holds `FxHashMap<IdentifierId, MutationKind>` (seen set) and `VecDeque<WorkItem>` (queue) that are cleared and reused across mutations instead of reallocating per mutation.
- Pre-sized hash maps: `ranges` and `creation_map` are pre-allocated based on total instruction count to reduce rehashing.
- Visitor-based operand ID collection: `annotate_last_use` uses `visit_operand_ids` callback pattern instead of `collect_operand_ids` which allocated a `Vec<IdentifierId>` per instruction.

**Benchmark results (p50, 100 iterations):**

| Fixture | Before | After | Improvement |
|---------|--------|-------|-------------|
| canvas-sidebar (272 LOC) | 248ms | 195ms | 21% |
| booking-list (152 LOC) | 72ms | 52ms | 28% |
| data-table (80 LOC) | 42ms | 27ms | 35% |

Zero conformance regressions (560/1717 maintained). All 103+ unit tests pass.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` | Sorted block processing, reused buffers, in-place merge, lightweight phi, terminal_successors_into |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges.rs` | Reusable BFS buffers, pre-sized maps, visitor-based operand IDs |

---

## Phase 177: Loop Codegen Fixes + Self-Assignment Stripping (555→557/1717, +2 conformance)

**Date:** 2026-04-05
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Group E loop codegen bugs
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/BuildReactiveFunction.ts`

Fixed all loop constructs (for, for-of, for-in, while, do-while) being silently dropped from compiler output. The root cause was in `build_scope_block_only` in `build_reactive_function.rs`: a catch-all `_ => {}` arm silently discarded any terminal that wasn't explicitly handled. Because reactive scopes typically inherit the terminal from the block they cover, and loop terminals (For, ForOf, ForIn, While, DoWhile, Label, Try) were not listed, any scope whose block ended in a loop would produce a scope wrapper with no body. Two commits addressed this across HIR lowering, the reactive tree builder, and codegen.

The first commit fixed the silent drop by adding explicit dispatch for every loop terminal in `build_scope_block_only`, and simultaneously improved while/do-while fidelity. `lower_while_statement` and `lower_do_while_statement` were changed to emit `Terminal::While` / `Terminal::DoWhile` directly instead of the previous `Goto + Branch` fallback. A new `build_loop_test_block` helper was added to extract the condition `Place` from the Branch terminal at the top of the test block. `ReactiveTerminal::While` and `ReactiveTerminal::DoWhile` gained a `condition: Option<Place>` field. Codegen emits `while (cond) {}` and `do {} while (cond)` respectively, with a `resolve_loop_condition` helper that looks up the condition place through the current scope's declarations. Five snapshots were rebased.

The second commit improved for-loop codegen to emit proper `for (init; cond; update)` syntax. `ReactiveTerminal::For` gained a `condition: Option<Place>` field mirroring the while change. The reactive tree builder gained `stop_at` boundary awareness for For sub-blocks so init/test/update are segmented correctly. Codegen uses new `codegen_for_init_expr` and `codegen_for_update_expr` helpers to produce the header. `merge_consecutive_blocks` was patched to recognize loop sub-block boundaries and avoid merging across them, which previously caused the test block to be absorbed into the init block. One known open issue remains: the for-loop update expression (e.g., `i++`) is eliminated by DCE in SSA because the SSA version it writes is never read — the phi-join at the loop header is not yet aware that the update block feeds back into the test block, so the write appears dead. Conformance was unchanged at 555/1717 from the loop commits alone because loop fixtures had other mismatches, but the behavioral change was significant: loops now appear in output instead of being silently dropped.

A third commit (+2 conformance, 555→557) addressed self-assignment pollution in codegen output. The scope body promotion step renames SSA temporaries to user variable names — e.g. temp `t5` is renamed to `items`, turning `t5 = items;` into `items = items;`. These spurious self-assignments were removed at three points: a `strip_self_assignments` post-processing step in `codegen_function` scrubs them from the final output string; the same stripping was added in `scope_body_replacements` where the rename happens; and an early guard was added in the `StoreLocal` handler to reject self-stores before they enter the output. Newly passing: `align-scopes-trycatch-nested-overlapping-range.ts` and `for-of-mutate-item-of-local-collection.js`.

A hook-validation fix was attempted but reverted. The change aimed to suppress the false-positive "Hooks may not be referenced as normal values" error for `PropertyLoad` on locally declared objects (e.g., `useFeature.useProperty`). The fix allowed a fixture to compile that should have bailed per upstream's intended behavior, causing a net -1 regression, so it was reverted before the session ended.

A minor refactor was also made: binary expressions in the inline map no longer wrap in `()` since the OXC normalizer handles operator precedence. No conformance change, but cleaner output.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/build_reactive_function.rs` | Added explicit loop terminal handlers in `build_scope_block_only`; added `build_loop_test_block` helper; `stop_at` boundary logic for For sub-blocks |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/types.rs` | Added `condition: Option<Place>` to `ReactiveTerminal::While`, `ReactiveTerminal::DoWhile`, and `ReactiveTerminal::For` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | Added `resolve_loop_condition` helper; loop emit fixes; `strip_self_assignments` post-processing in `codegen_function`; early self-assignment guard in `StoreLocal` handler; removed unnecessary `()` wrapping on inlined binary expressions |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/build.rs` | `lower_while_statement` and `lower_do_while_statement` emit `Terminal::While`/`Terminal::DoWhile` instead of `Goto + Branch` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/optimization/merge_consecutive_blocks.rs` | Prevented merging across loop sub-block boundaries |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/scope_body_replacements.rs` | Added self-assignment stripping after temp-to-user-name rename |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/snapshots/fixture_tests__hook-with-state_tsx.snap` | Rebased after loop codegen change |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__hook_dependencies.snap` | Rebased after loop codegen change |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/snapshots/snapshot_tests__e2e_memoization.snap` | Rebased after loop codegen change |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/snapshots/snapshot_tests__hook_component.snap` | Rebased after loop codegen change |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/snapshots/snapshot_tests__hook_with_use_state.snap` | Rebased after loop codegen change |

## Phase 176: Fixture-driven debugging + sentinel dep pruning (229/566, +1 slot-MATCH)

**Date:** 2026-04-04
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 3 — Apply resolution and mutation propagation (566 slot-DIFFER fixtures)
**Upstream:** N/A (OXC-specific optimization)

Added temporary debug output to the conformance test harness to enumerate all 52 surplus-scope (+1) fixtures with exact slot counts, then manually debugged four representative cases to categorize the root causes. Three distinct categories emerged. First, loop codegen bugs (~12 fixtures): `do-while-simple.js` shows the do-while loop body is flattened in codegen so the loop body falls outside the reactive scope; `for-of-simple.js` is more severe — the for-of loop body is completely absent from codegen output, meaning the scope wraps nothing. These are codegen structural issues unrelated to scope inference. Second, unnecessary dep scopes for sentinel-stable values: `hooks-freeze-arguments.js` creates a dep scope for `call(a)` where `a` is a function argument declared as sentinel-cached — the scope can never invalidate because sentinel values are immutable across renders. Third, redundant scope declarations: `ssa-non-empty-initializer.js` stores both `x` and `y` when `y = x` is a simple alias, creating two scope declarations where one suffices.

The actionable fix was implementing `prune_scopes_with_sentinel_only_deps` in `prune_scopes.rs`. The pass iterates all reactive scopes and checks whether every dep in the scope's dependency set is declared via a sentinel instruction (i.e., a function parameter with a stable identity, hook return values marked immutable, or similar). If all deps are sentinel-stable, the scope can never actually invalidate, so it is safe to unwrap — removing the scope guard and inlining its instructions. The pass was wired into `pipeline.rs` immediately after the existing `prune_always_invalidating_scopes` pass (both passes reduce scope count; placing sentinel pruning after always-invalidating pruning avoids re-examining scopes that were already eliminated). Result: +1 slot-MATCH (228→229), -1 slot-DIFFER (566→565), zero regressions. The loop codegen bugs remain open as a separate work item.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/prune_scopes.rs` | Added `prune_scopes_with_sentinel_only_deps` pass — unwraps scopes whose entire dep set consists of sentinel-declared values |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Wired `prune_scopes_with_sentinel_only_deps` after `prune_always_invalidating_scopes` |

---

## Phase 175: Stage 3 scope inference divergence investigation — root cause analysis, no code changes (555/1717, +0)

**Date:** 2026-04-04
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 3 — Apply resolution and mutation propagation (566 slot-DIFFER fixtures)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingRanges.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`

Conducted a deep-work diagnostic session targeting the 566 slot-DIFFER fixtures. The goal was to determine whether our mutation aliasing pipeline (effects → ranges → scope inference) was architecturally aligned with upstream, or whether structural gaps remained. No code was committed; the working tree is clean at session end.

The first phase of the session confirmed that the three pipeline stages are architecturally sound. `aliasing_effects.rs` computes candidate effects matching upstream's `computeSignatureForInstruction`. `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` contains a full abstract interpreter with `InferenceState` (value kinds, pointer sets), three-tier Apply resolution, and mutation refinement. `infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges.rs` has graph-based BFS mutation propagation matching upstream's algorithm. One important stale comment was identified: line 507 of `infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges.rs` has `// DIVERGENCE: Apply should be resolved by analyse_functions but we don't have that pass yet` — this comment is incorrect; the effects pass that resolves Apply does exist. The `Apply { .. } => {}` skip at that site is correct behavior, not a missing implementation.

The second phase identified four concrete divergences in `infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs` and tested two of them. **Rank 1 (highest impact):** the `effective_range = max(mutable_range.end, last_use + 1)` workaround causes over-merging; upstream uses raw `mutable_range`. Switching `use_mutable_range=true` causes -40 conformance regressions because our mutable ranges are still slightly narrower than upstream's — the workaround compensates for this deficit. **Rank 2:** the missing `mutableRange.start > 0` guard on operands was tested — it causes a net -2 slot MATCH regression because it prevents legitimate operand merges that the system currently relies on via the effective_range dependency. **Rank 3:** our `any_reactive && any_mutable` pre-filter gates scope creation, whereas upstream creates ALL sets as scopes and prunes later. **Rank 4:** missing `is_allocating_instruction` cases (PropertyStore, ComputedStore, spread Destructure) — testing PropertyStore showed +1 MATCH but also caused global property stores (`wat.test = 1`) to create scopes that prevent global mutation bail-outs, netting +1/-1.

The session concluded that all four individual fixes create cascading regressions because they interact with the `effective_range` workaround. Each fix is individually correct (matching upstream's logic) but our pipeline has compensating errors — removing any one mechanism breaks the balance. The correct sequencing is: (1) ensure `infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges` produces ranges matching upstream exactly, (2) switch to `use_mutable_range=true`, (3) apply the scope inference fixes in order. Step 1 is the prerequisite. The ranges algorithm is structurally correct, so the remaining inaccuracy likely comes from subtle differences in the abstract interpreter's value-kind tracking or the Apply resolution's conservative fallback, not a missing structural component.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| *(none — investigation only, all experimental code reverted before session end)* | |

---

## Phase 174: validate_no_unsupported_nodes + validate_no_mutation_after_freeze — 2 more error fixtures (+2, 553→555)

**Date:** 2026-04-04
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 4f Group D simple (2 fixtures)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateNoUnsupportedSyntax.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateNoMutationAfterFreeze.ts`

Two independent validation fixes, each unblocking one previously failing fixture.

The first fix rewrote `check_update_context_identifiers` in `validate_no_unsupported_nodes.rs`. The old approach checked for `LoadContext`/`StoreContext` instruction markers, which our HIR builder never emits for nested function environments — only `LoadLocal`/`StoreLocal` are used. The new approach uses name-based matching: collect all `DeclareLocal`/`StoreLocal` lvalue names from the outer function body, then scan inner lambdas for `PrefixUpdate`/`PostfixUpdate` instructions whose lvalue name appears in the outer set. To prevent false positives from shadowing, any name declared inside the inner function (including its parameters) is excluded from the match set. This correctly detects `counter++` on outer-scope variables like `let counter = 0` inside nested lambdas, matching the upstream pattern (`error.todo-handle-update-context-identifiers.js`).

The second fix added "Check 6" to `validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` — detection of frozen context variable reassignment in for-loop updaters. The pattern is a `StoreLocal { Reassign }` instruction whose lvalue name appears in both `frozen_names` (established by a prior freeze) and `closure_captured_names` (a new set built by scanning `MakeObject`/`MakeArray`/`CallExpression`/`MethodCall` operands for names used inside closure bodies). A critical ordering guard (`frozen_at[name] < instr.id`) ensures the freeze instruction precedes the reassignment; without this guard, an initial false-positive regression appeared in `hoisting-reassigned-let-declaration` (where `let x; x += 1; <JSX getX={getX}>` has the JSX freeze appearing AFTER the reassignment — without ordering verification, Check 6 incorrectly bailed on the reassignment). The `InstructionKind` import was added to support the `Reassign` variant match. Newly passing fixture: `error.todo-for-loop-with-context-variable-iterator.js`.

A third fixture (`error.bug-invariant-unnamed-temporary`) was investigated but left unimplemented. Upstream's invariant fires when a temporary lacks a user-visible name. Our `promote_used_temporaries` pass blanket-assigns names to all temporaries, making the invariant condition unreachable without restructuring the promotion pass — documented for future work.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_unsupported_nodes.rs` | Rewrote `check_update_context_identifiers` to use name-based outer/inner scope matching instead of LoadContext/StoreContext markers |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` | Added Check 6 (frozen context variable reassignment in for-loop updaters), `closure_captured_names` set, `InstructionKind` import, `frozen_at` ordering guard |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 2 newly-passing fixtures |

## Phase 173: effective_range investigation — Apply processing tested, balance problem identified (553/1717, +0)

**Date:** 2026-04-03
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 3b (scope inference) — mutable range accuracy / effective_range divergence
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingRanges.ts`

Investigated the effective_range divergence — the largest single remaining divergence in scope inference. The effective_range in our system extends a value's range to cover its last use (`max(mutable_range, last_use)`), which is a workaround for missing upstream mutation propagation logic. Three approaches were tested to narrow or correct this workaround, all reverted.

Approach 1 extended stored value's `mutable_range` to cover the `StoreLocal` instruction in `infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges.rs`, matching an existing `StoreContext` fix. Result: neutral conformance but -10 slot accuracy (238→228 MATCH). Ranges became too wide, causing over-merging of scopes. Approach 2 implemented minimal Apply effect handling — creating conditional mutations for args and `CreateFrom` edges from args to the return value. Result: same -10 slot accuracy shift. The graph edges were too aggressive, producing the same over-merging pattern. Approach 3 retested `use_mutable_range=true` with the `is_mutable` fix from Phase 172 already in place. Result: still -40 regression. Mutable ranges remain too narrow without last_use extension even with reduced is_mutable scope.

The core balance problem is now confirmed: widening (Apply processing, StoreLocal extension) and narrowing (use_mutable_range) both cause regressions. The current `effective_range = max(mutable_range, last_use)` is the best available approximation, but still leaves ~572 slot-DIFFER surplus. Fixing it requires upstream's exact Apply resolution logic — how signatures are resolved, which edges are created, and how propagation depth is limited. Apply effects are completely skipped (`AliasingEffect::Apply { .. } => {}`) in our range inference; correct handling requires understanding upstream's `SignatureModel` and Apply resolution pipeline, not a local approximation. All experimental code was reverted; working tree is clean.

---

## Phase 172: First successful scope inference fix (+3, 550→553)

**Date:** 2026-04-03
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 3b (scope inference) — reduce scope surplus
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/AliasingEffects.ts`

Two targeted scope inference changes drawn from deep upstream comparison, yielding the first successful scope fix after 6 prior failed approaches across 3 sessions.

The first change (in `aliasing_effects.rs`) revised the mutation effect applied to unknown-method receivers: changed `MutateTransitiveConditionally` to `MutateConditionally`. This prevents the receiver's mutable range from extending through the full alias graph, producing a safer and more accurate mutation model. The change is conformance-neutral on its own but corrects the aliasing semantics.

The second change (in `infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs`) excludes `CallExpression` and `MethodCall` results from the `is_mutable_instruction` predicate. Previously these instruction kinds were treated as unconditional allocations, causing the `any_reactive && any_mutable` condition to trigger scope creation for any reactive+call instruction set. Upstream only considers literal allocations mutable for scope creation purposes: `ObjectExpression`, `ArrayExpression`, JSX, `NewExpression`, and `FunctionExpression`. Removing `CallExpression`/`MethodCall` from the mutable category brought +3 conformance. Three fixtures that had been in `known-failures.txt` now pass: `rules-of-hooks/rules-of-hooks-23dc7fffde57.js`, `template-literal.js`, and `unknown-hooks-do-not-assert.js`.

Two additional approaches were investigated but reverted. Removing the `last_use > instr_id` gate produced a -5 regression (more sentinel scopes created than needed). Setting `use_mutable_range=true` combined with the `is_mutable` fix produced a -40 regression (mutable ranges are still too narrow to be used alone). All reverted code was removed cleanly before committing.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/aliasing_effects.rs` | Unknown MethodCall receiver mutation: `MutateTransitiveConditionally` → `MutateConditionally` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs` | Exclude `CallExpression` and `MethodCall` from `is_mutable_instruction` predicate |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 3 newly-passing fixtures |

---

## Phase 171: Scope inference investigation — all approaches blocked by scope surplus (550/1717, +0)

**Date:** 2026-04-03
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 3b (scope inference) — scope surplus root cause investigation
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependencies.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidatePreservedManualMemoization.ts`

Investigated how to improve scope inference to unblock the preserve-memo path. Four distinct implementation approaches were tried across all three files, all reverted, conformance unchanged at 550/1717.

Approach 1 propagated scopes to `FinishMemoize.decl.identifier` in Phase 5 of `infer_reactive_scope_variables`: bails dropped 94→14 (correct), but introduced a -52 conformance regression. Root cause: 52 error fixtures have scopes in our system that upstream doesn't create — these fixtures pass Check 1 (scope exists, completed) when they should fail. Approach 2 built a `scope_ranges` map in Phase 2 of `propagate_dependencies` and used range-based lookup to assign scopes to unscoped instructions (`LoadLocal`, `PropertyLoad`) inside scope ranges. Individually neutral. Combined with scope propagation: still -52. Approach 3 changed Check 1 in `validate_preserved_manual_memoization` to match upstream `isUnmemoized` semantics (`None → false`). Individually -56, combined with approaches 1+2 still -52. All three together still yielded the same -52 net. The root cause is confirmed at the deepest level: **scope surplus**. Our scope inference creates reactive scopes for `CallExpression` results (useMemo return values) that upstream does NOT scope. These are the same ~572 fixtures causing slot-DIFFER divergence. No combination of dep-collection or validation fixes can compensate for incorrect scope creation. Phase 2 of `propagate_dependencies` only collects deps from scoped instructions (`lvalue.identifier.scope = Some`); intermediate instructions (`LoadLocal`, `PropertyLoad`) inside scope ranges get `scope=None` and are skipped — many scopes therefore have zero named-variable deps. This investigation (21 total approaches across 4 sessions: 10 dep-resolution, 6 scope-inference, 3 scope-propagation, 2 validation) confirms that **scope surplus is the single gating bottleneck**. All remaining conformance gains require reducing surplus scopes via the Stage 3 prerequisites: mutable range accuracy, receiver mutation effects, dep.reactive audit.

---

## Phase 170: Check 1 investigation — root cause is scope assignment, not pruning (550/1717, +0)

**Date:** 2026-04-03
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 4b (preserve-memo validation) — Check 1 false bails
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidatePreservedManualMemoization.ts` — `isUnmemoized()`

After Phase 169 shifted all 194 preserve-memo bails from Check 2 to Check 1, this session investigated whether Check 1 bails could be fixed in validation. Three distinct approaches were attempted and all reverted; conformance stayed at 550/1717.

The first approach modified `prune_non_escaping_scopes` and `prune_unused_scopes` to return pruned scope IDs, threaded them into validation via `pipeline.rs`, and added them to `completed_scopes` in `WalkerState`. Result: zero impact — none of the 194 bailing `FinishMemoize` declarations had scopes that were pruned. The second approach changed Check 1 to match upstream's `isUnmemoized` semantics — returning `false` (not unmemoized) when `decl_scope_id` is `None`. Result: net regression of -56: 84 fewer false bails but 56 error fixtures that previously bailed via `None → true` (accidental correctness) now compile through and diverge from upstream. The root cause analysis then identified the real problem: **all 194 Check 1 bails have `decl_scope_id = None`** — the FinishMemoize decl identifier has no scope at all, meaning `infer_reactive_scope_variables` never assigned a scope to that identifier. Upstream assigns scopes to these identifiers and then checks them; our code has no scope to check. The 56 "load-bearing" bails are cases where upstream assigns a scope, checks it, finds it incomplete, and bails for a correct reason — we achieve the same bail accidentally via `None → true`. Fixing the 94 net-false bails requires scope inference to assign scopes to FinishMemoize decl targets, which is Stage 3b territory. All experimental code was reverted.

---

## Phase 169: Breakthrough — unnamed dep skip eliminates all Check 2 bails

**Date:** 2026-04-03
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 4b (preserve-memo validation) — dep resolution
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependencies.ts` — `propagateScopeDependencies()` else-branch

Skipping unnamed SSA temporaries (`name == None`) in the Phase 2 else-branch of `propagate_scope_dependencies_hir` completely eliminated all Check 2 bails in `validate_preserved_manual_memoization`. The fix is a pre-naming filter applied at dep-collection time — before `promote_used_temporaries` assigns synthetic `tN` names — making it safe where a post-naming filter was previously confirmed harmful (Approach 6, -55). The key insight from Phase 167's investigation: the correct intervention point is dep-collection, not dep-resolution. When a temp has no user-visible name at collection time, it should not be stored as a scope dep at all. This is the first positive infrastructure change in a series of 9 failed approaches.

Conformance stayed at 550/1717 but slot accuracy improved: +3 fixtures moved from DIFFER to MATCH (238 vs 235 previously). Check 2 bails dropped from 154 to 0; Check 1 bails rose from 0 to 194. The preserve-memo bail count remains 94 fixtures total, but all now originate from Check 1 (scope inference gaps — scopes not created or incorrectly pruned), which is a different and more tractable problem than dep resolution. The blocker has shifted from "dep resolution" to "scope inference," enabling Stage 3b liveness range work to unblock the remaining preserve-memo failures.

Also removed a stale DIVERGENCE comment in `validate_preserved_manual_memoization.rs` that had been added during Phase 163's failed tN-skip experiment, since that workaround is now obsolete.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | Phase 2 else-branch: skip deps where `identifier.name.is_none()` before storing as scope dep |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_preserved_manual_memoization.rs` | Removed stale DIVERGENCE comment about SSA temp skipping |

## Phase 168: Stage 4f investigation — all remaining tractable items blocked (550/1717, +0)

**Date:** 2026-04-03
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 4f (bail-out sweep)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependencies.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/HIR/BuildHIR.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidatePreservedManualMemoization.ts`

Systematically investigated all remaining Stage 4f tractable items: 7 "Found 1 error:" fixtures in the "We compile, they don't" category, 9 silent bail-outs, and 3 different implementation approaches. Every attempt either compiled clean with zero conformance impact or was outright harmful, and all code was reverted. Conformance stayed at 550/1717.

The 7 "Found 1 error:" fixtures are all blocked at the infrastructure level. `error.bug-invariant-unnamed-temporary.js` would require adding a semantically incorrect upstream bug-invariant check. The two JSX capture fixtures (`error.invalid-jsx-captures-context-variable.js` and `error.todo-handle-update-context-identifiers.js`) and two for-loop context-variable fixtures are blocked on LoadContext/context-variable detection in nested HIR — missing infrastructure. The two `repro-preserve-memo-*` fixtures are blocked on the scope dep resolution gap (the same root cause as Phase 167). The `new-mutability/error.mutate-frozen-value` fixture requires both `@enableNewMutationAliasingModel` and a `useFreeze` intrinsic, neither implemented. All 9 silent bail-outs are scope inference gaps (0 scopes created), not validation gaps — fixing them requires the Stage 3b liveness range work.

Three implementation approaches were attempted and reverted. First: adding `collect_destructure_target_places` in `propagate_scope_dependencies_hir` Phase 3 to extract named targets from Destructure patterns as scope declarations — compiled clean, zero impact because scope inference doesn't create scopes for the target fixture (`unused-object-element-with-rest.js`). Second: removing the `lvalue.identifier.name.is_none()` guard in the Phase 1.5 StoreLocal handler to match upstream's `collectTemporaries` — compiled clean, zero impact because StoreLocal instruction result IDs are never read by other instructions. Third: enhancing the `temp_map` in Phase 1.5 to resolve MethodCall results to their receiver and CallExpression results to their callee — compiled clean but HARMFUL: resolving previously-skipped `tN` deps into named deps created MORE `validateInferredDep` mismatches (bail count stayed at 199 but shifted 18 fixtures between categories), confirming that `resolve_scope_dep` in validation skips `None` (unresolvable) deps but flags named deps that don't match the source. The fix must change what deps are collected at dep-collection time, not how they are resolved downstream.

## Phase 167: tN dep resolution deep investigation (550/1717, +0)

**Date:** 2026-04-03
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 4b (preserve-memo validation) — dep resolution
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependencies.ts` — `collectTemporaries()`, `propagateScopeDependencies()`

Conducted a systematic investigation into why 76 preserve-memo fixtures produce Check 2 (dep mismatch) false bails, specifically why scope deps appear as synthetic `tN` names (e.g. `t11`) rather than named variables. The investigation was scoped and experimental — all code was reverted at the end; conformance stayed at 550/1717.

The first step was producer attribution: added debug instrumentation to classify which instruction kinds generate the unresolvable `tN` deps. Result: `StoreLocal` is the dominant producer at 1553/3588 (43%), not `CallExpression` or `MethodCall` as previously assumed. The pattern is `StoreLocal x = $result_from_outside_scope` where `$result` has no entry in `temp_map` because its `LoadLocal` was inlined away before the temp map was built. A "defining_operands" tracing approach was then prototyped: build an `IdentifierId → Vec<OperandId>` map from HIR, then for each unresolved `tN` dep, walk back through its defining instruction's read operands to find a named root. This required three new constructs added to `validate_preserved_manual_memoization.rs` (`DefiningOperandsMap` type, `build_defining_operands_map_hir`, `build_defining_operands_map_rf`, `resolve_through_defining_operands`) and a pipeline change in `pipeline.rs` to build and thread the map through. The `propagate_dependencies.rs` else-branch was also patched to attempt recursive resolution before storing a dep. However, the trace results exposed a semantic gap: of 76 traces attempted, 15 found a named root and 61 found none (those terminated at `Primitive`, `LoadGlobal`, or `FunctionExpression` — truly opaque instructions). Of the 15 successes, 0 matched the user's source dep array. The traced root is often an INPUT to the computation (e.g. `onFoo`), while upstream's dep is the named INPUT it resolves to via a different path (e.g. `props`).

The investigation confirmed three facts. First, `collectTemporaries()` in upstream covers more patterns than our current temp_map: specifically, `StoreLocal` propagation (if `x = $t`, then `$t` resolves to whatever `x` resolves to) and possibly `MethodCall` receiver chains. Second, the "defining_operands" backward-trace approach is structurally correct but semantically insufficient — even a successful trace produces the wrong named root because we're recovering an input to a computation rather than the dep the user listed. Third, the correct fix must happen at dep collection time in `propagate_scope_dependencies_hir`: when a scope dep is added via the else-branch, resolve it forward-to-named before storing, so the stored dep matches what upstream would have stored. All experimental code was reverted cleanly (`git status` confirmed clean tree).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | (reverted) Attempted recursive resolution in else-branch when adding scope deps |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_preserved_manual_memoization.rs` | (reverted) Added `DefiningOperandsMap` type, `build_defining_operands_map_hir`, `build_defining_operands_map_rf`, `resolve_through_defining_operands`, debug tracing in `validate_scope_deps` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | (reverted) Added building and passing of `defining_operands` map through pipeline |

---

## Phase 166: Scope completion tracking in validate_preserved_manual_memoization (550/1717, +1)

**Date:** 2026-04-03
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 4b (preserve-memo validation)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidatePreservedManualMemoization.ts` — `Visitor.scopes: Set<ScopeId>` and `isUnmemoized()`

Replaced the old `finish_in_scope: bool` flag in `WalkerState` with upstream's correct post-order scope completion tracking using `completed_scopes: FxHashSet<ScopeId>`. The old flag was set lexically (whether `FinishMemoize` was inside a `ReactiveInstruction::Scope` arm), which was wrong: it didn't account for sibling or ancestor scopes that had already completed. The fix adds a post-order insertion in `walk_reactive_block` — after traversing a scope's children, both `scope.id` and all merged scope IDs are inserted into `completed_scopes`. Check 1 then queries `completed_scopes.contains(&scope_id)` instead of tracking an `in_scope` boolean through recursion. The `in_scope` parameter was removed from `walk_reactive_block`, `check_instruction`, and `walk_terminal_blocks`. `MemoRegion.finish_in_scope: bool` was replaced with `MemoRegion.decl_scope_id: Option<ScopeId>`, storing only the scope ID rather than a full `Identifier` clone. One DIVERGENCE note was added: upstream checks all `FinishMemoize` operands for scope completion, but we only check the decl's scope (sufficient for the one newly passing fixture). Removed `useCallback-ref-in-render.js` from `known-failures.txt`.

The session also included a deep investigation into the remaining 76 preserve-memo false bails (all Check 2 — dep mismatch, not Check 1). Debug logging across all 154 bailing functions confirmed `check1_count=0` universally. The mismatching deps are all synthetic `tN` names (e.g. `t11`) produced by `promote_used_temporaries` using `format!("t{}", identifier.id.0)`. Of these, 55 are load-bearing: upstream also bails on those fixtures but for a correct reason (genuine dep mismatch or unmemoized value), so naively skipping `tN` deps causes a -55 regression. The root cause is that computation-result temps (from `CallExpression`, `ArrayExpression`, etc.) are not captured in the pre-inline temp map because their `LoadLocal` was inlined away. Resolving this requires tracing computation-result temps back to their source variable deps — either by enhancing the temp map, building a reverse dep map, or having `propagate_dependencies.rs` produce named deps. Blocked on significant infrastructure work.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_preserved_manual_memoization.rs` | Added `completed_scopes: FxHashSet<ScopeId>` to `WalkerState`; replaced `MemoRegion.finish_in_scope` with `decl_scope_id: Option<ScopeId>`; post-order scope completion in `walk_reactive_block`; removed `in_scope` parameter from `walk_reactive_block`/`check_instruction`/`walk_terminal_blocks`; updated Check 1 to use `completed_scopes.contains`; added DIVERGENCE note; fixed duplicate doc comment on `build_temporaries_map_from_hir` |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed `useCallback-ref-in-render.js` (newly passing) |

## Phase 164: Try-catch value block bail-out (536/1717, +10)

**Date:** 2026-04-03
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 4f (bail-out sweep)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/HIR/BuildHIR.ts` — `lowerStatement` / try-catch handling

Added AST-level detection of "value blocks" inside `try` statement bodies. Upstream bails with a `Todo` when a `try` block contains expressions that create complex control flow — specifically optional chaining (`OptionalMemberExpression`, `OptionalCallExpression`), nullish coalescing (`??`), logical expressions (`&&`, `||`), conditional expressions (`? :`), and loop constructs (`for-in`, `for-of`, `for`). These constructs require value block semantics that are incompatible with the try/catch HIR model. Three new functions were added to `build.rs`: `try_block_has_value_blocks` iterates top-level statements in the try block, `try_stmt_has_value_block` dispatches over statement kinds, and `try_expr_has_value_block` recursively checks expressions. The bail-out identifier `TryStatement_value_blocks` was registered in `REJECTED_UNSUPPORTED_NODES`. Removed 10 fixtures from `known-failures.txt`.

## Phase 162: Infer-mode body heuristic — body_has_hooks_or_jsx shallow AST walk (496/1717, +4)

**Date:** 2026-04-03
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 3b (Infer-mode body heuristic)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Entrypoint/Program.ts` — `hasHooksOrJsx` function and its usage in `filterCompileTargets`

Added the `body_has_hooks_or_jsx` heuristic to `CompilationMode::Infer` in `should_compile` and `should_compile_default_export`. The heuristic performs a shallow AST walk over a function's body statements, detecting hook calls (identifiers starting with `use`) and JSX elements, without descending into nested function expressions or arrow functions. This matches upstream's `hasHooksOrJsx` which skips compiling functions in Infer mode that contain neither hooks nor JSX — those functions are not React components or hooks and should be left alone. Three new helper functions implement the walk: `stmt_has_hooks_or_jsx` dispatches over statement kinds, `expr_has_hooks_or_jsx` handles expressions including `ConditionalExpression` test-branch checking and `LogicalExpression`, and `call_is_hook` / `is_hook_name` identify hook calls by the `use`-prefix naming convention. Both `should_compile` and `should_compile_default_export` were updated to accept `body_stmts: Option<&[Statement<'_>]>` and return early with `false` when the body is present and contains no hooks or JSX; all 8 call sites were updated accordingly. A pre-existing clippy warning (single-arm `match` → `if let`) was also fixed in the same pass.

The session also reconciled a state discrepancy: the previous session had left `program.rs` and `known-failures.txt` with uncommitted changes that were out of sync — `known-failures.txt` had been partially updated but the corresponding code changes were not committed. This session incorporated those pre-existing changes, added the Infer heuristic on top, and performed a full reconciliation pass on `known-failures.txt`: 24 fixtures removed (21 from the pre-existing uncommitted delta, 3 specifically fixed by the Infer heuristic — `dont-memoize-primitive-function-call-non-escaping.js`, `infer-no-component-nested-jsx.js`, `infer-skip-components-without-hooks-or-jsx.js`), and 38 new divergences added (pre-existing regressions from prior uncommitted changes that had never been synced to the failure list). Net conformance: 492→496 matched (+4), 1225→1221 diverged.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/program.rs` | Added `body_has_hooks_or_jsx`, `stmt_has_hooks_or_jsx`, `expr_has_hooks_or_jsx`, `call_is_hook`, `is_hook_name` helpers; updated `should_compile` and `should_compile_default_export` to accept `body_stmts: Option<&[Statement<'_>]>` and bail when body has no hooks or JSX in Infer mode; fixed clippy single-arm match warning; updated all 8 call sites |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Reconciled to current state: removed 24 now-passing fixtures (21 pre-existing, 3 from Infer heuristic), added 38 new divergences (pre-existing regressions synced for first time) |

## Phase 161: Stage 3b scope inference merging — deep-work session, all approaches net-negative, reverted (507/1717, +0)

**Date:** 2026-03-26
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 3b (scope inference merging)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/HIR/PruneNonReactiveDeps.ts`

A full deep-work session targeting Stage 3b — scope inference merging, which drives 666 SLOTS-DIFFER fixtures (53% of all failures). The session was structured in three planned steps: (1) switch operand liveness from `effective_range` to `mutable_range`, (2) fix scope range for pure sentinels, (3) implement `prune_non_reactive_deps`. All three were implemented and tested; all produced net-negative results and were reverted. Conformance remains at 507/1717.

Step 1a (blanket operand liveness switch) changed `infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs` Phase 2 (lines 148–174) to use `mutable_range` for all liveness decisions instead of `effective_range`. Result: -24 net (2 gains, 26 regressions). Our `mutable_range` values are systematically narrower than upstream's, so any instruction whose operand spans `effective_range > mutable_range` loses its liveness extension — the scope is created too early or not created at all, breaking slot counts. Step 1b narrowed the change to allocating-instructions only (`is_allocating_instruction` gate preserved, switch applies only inside that branch). Result: -17 net (0 gains, 17 regressions). Still net-negative for the same root cause. Step 1c experimented with 0-slot codegen: functions where `has_cache_slots` is false (`entrypoint/program.rs` lines 485–490) were made to emit source-reconstructed output instead of IR-reconstructed output. Result: -51 net. The IR-reconstructed codegen for 0-slot functions produces fundamentally different textual formatting (statement ordering, temp variable insertion) from the original source text, so fixtures that were passing with the existing 0-slot path all regressed. Step 3 implemented `prune_non_reactive_deps_in_block` in `prune_scopes.rs` (lines 813–828), marking dep entries as non-reactive when the dep identifier has no reactive scope. Result: -107 net. The `dep.reactive` flag in our implementation does not have the same semantics as upstream's: many deps are flagged non-reactive but are still consumed by codegen to emit the correct `$[...]` slot reads, so removing them collapses entire cache blocks.

The core finding from the session is that all three planned improvements share the same prerequisite: `infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges.rs` must produce wider `mutable_range` values matching upstream before any downstream liveness switch is safe. Two specific gaps in that file cause the systematic narrowness: (a) `MethodCall` Apply effects do not propagate mutation to the receiver (upstream does this via `apply_effect` on the receiver for `mutate` effects), and (b) there is no reverse scope propagation — upstream walks scopes in reverse and extends the range of any variable whose scope's `range.end` exceeds the variable's current `mutable_range.end`. Until both are fixed, operand liveness switches are blocked. The `dep.reactive` semantics issue is a separate blocker for `prune_non_reactive_deps` and requires investigation of how upstream's `InferReactiveScopeVariables` sets that flag versus our implementation. These findings are recorded as prerequisites in `.todo/index.md`.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `.todo/index.md` | Stage 3b prerequisites documented: receiver mutation effects and reverse scope propagation in `infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges.rs`; `dep.reactive` semantics investigation noted |

---

## Phase 160: Gating directive stripping, hook-as-value false positive fix, bail-out diagnostics (507/1717, +2)

**Date:** 2026-03-26
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 1d (codegen polish); Stage 4e (validation hardening)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Codegen/CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateHooksUsage.ts`

Three improvements were shipped in this continuation session, netting +2 conformance (505→507/1717).

First, `codegen.rs` gained filtering of `// @gating` and `// @dynamicGating` comment lines from compiled output when gating mode is active. The upstream compiler strips these directive comments before emitting; the OXC codegen was previously preserving them, causing two fixtures to produce spurious comment lines. The fix iterates over leading comments on each statement and suppresses lines whose trimmed content starts with `@gating` or `@dynamicGating`. Trailing newline preservation was also corrected to avoid producing a double blank line at end-of-output. Second, `validate_hooks_usage.rs` gained `locally_declared_names` — a `HashSet<CompactStr>` populated by walking `DeclareLocal` and `Destructure` instructions (the latter via a new `collect_destructure_names` helper that recursively extracts all bound names from `DestructurePattern`). Rule 3 (hooks-as-values check) now skips `LoadLocal` of any name present in the set, preventing false bails on patterns like `let useFeature = makeObject()`. No net conformance change from this fix alone — the 3 affected fixtures are still caught by the `PropertyLoad` callee-name check which is a separate issue, so the hook-as-value fix is a correctness improvement with zero net score change. Third, `conformance_tests.rs` gained per-fixture name display in the bail-out breakdown diagnostic, making it possible to trace which specific test is responsible for each bail-out category.

Four reverted experiments produced zero net change: removing the recursive ref check (-9 regression), removing `check_nested_method_call_as_argument` (-2 regression), removing the `is_allocating_instruction` last_use gate in scope inference (-5 regression), and modifications to the `PropertyLoad` hook-name check (net zero).

## Phase 159: Stage 3b scope inference investigation — failed experiments, silent bail-out root cause, SLOTS-MATCH systemic analysis (505→505/1717)

**Date:** 2026-03-26
**Task:** .todo/bail-out-investigation.md -- Stage 3b (scope inference under-creating); .todo/index.md -- Stage 3b backlog
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/HIR/MergeOverlappingReactiveScopes.ts`

A deep-work investigation session targeting the 505→600 gap. No code changes were shipped; all experiments were reverted. The session produced three findings about why incremental scope inference improvements are blocked and what the systemic barriers to reaching 600+ are.

The first experiment removed the `last_use > instr_id` guard from `is_allocating_instruction` in `infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs`, the known Stage 3b root cause. Net result: -5 (505→500). The extra sentinel-range scopes created by the change survive `infer_reactive_scope_variables` but then get merged with existing scopes by `merge_overlapping_reactive_scopes_hir`, which inflates cache slot counts for fixtures that were previously generating correct output. The union-find over-merging is the real blocker; fixing the liveness gate in isolation makes things worse by feeding more merge candidates into the over-eager merge pass. Reverted.

The second experiment removed the `check_nested_method_call_as_argument` bail-out added in Phase 157. Net result: -2 (505→503). The 6 fixtures that bail via that check would, without the bail, produce incorrect codegen that over-counts cache slots, causing those fixtures to regress from pass to fail. The bail-outs are not just correct — they are actively preventing worse divergence. Kept as-is.

The third area was analysis of the 8 "silent bail-out" fixtures — functions that produce 0 scopes where upstream produces scopes. Root cause is confirmed as the same Stage 3b issue: `is_allocating_instruction` misses ranges where the variable's last use is at the instruction that defines it (e.g., a value used only as an argument and never stored). No fix attempted.

A structural analysis of the 238 SLOTS-MATCH fixtures (output structure identical, slot counts match, but variable names/declaration placement differ) identified three dominant patterns: (1) temp variable names (`t0`, `t1`, ...) where upstream uses original source names — requires the `named-variable-preservation` work tracked separately; (2) separate `let x; x = val` declaration/initialization versus upstream's inline `let x = val` — a codegen placement issue in `ReactiveFunction` lowering; (3) scope boundary ordering differences where two scopes cover the same range but are emitted in different order. All three are systemic codegen issues requiring multi-session effort; none yield to targeted fixes. The key finding is that reaching 600+ from 505 requires either scope inference repair (high risk, blocked by over-merging) or systemic codegen normalization (variable naming, declaration placement). Both are multi-session projects with significant regression risk.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `.todo/index.md` | Updated conformance stats, Stage 2g completion notes, backlog priorities (taskmaster agent) |
| `.todo/bail-out-investigation.md` | Stage 2g section with all four bail-out fixes documented; 0-slot codegen rejection documented (taskmaster agent) |

## Phase 158: Stage 2g error.* bail-out sweep — fbt duplicate tags, ref-to-function, self-referencing const, dynamic gating validation (+6, 499→505/1717)

**Date:** 2026-03-26
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 2g (error fixture bail-out sweep)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateNoRefAccessInRender.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/EnterSSA/EnterSSA.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/HIR/Program.ts`

Four new validation bail-outs were added across three files, each targeting a distinct class of error fixtures. The net gain was +6 conformance (499→505/1717).

First, `validate_no_unsupported_nodes.rs` gained `check_fbt_duplicate_tags` — a two-pass analysis that first collects all fbt/fbs identifiers referenced in a function via `LoadLocal`/`LoadContext`/`LoadGlobal` (noting that `import fbt from 'fbt'` creates a `LoadLocal` not `LoadGlobal` because fbt is absent from the built-in globals list), then counts `_enum`/`_plural`/`_pronoun` MethodCall sub-tags per identifier. If any tag type appears two or more times on the same fbt/fbs root, the function bails. This fixes the two duplicate-fbt-tag error fixtures (+2). The same file also gained `check_self_referencing_declarations` which detects `const x = identity(x)` — a `LoadLocal` referencing the same `IdentifierId` before the matching `StoreLocal` within the same declaration block. The implementation walks instructions in reverse to find a `StoreLocal` for each `LoadLocal`, stopping at `DeclareLocal`/`Destructure` boundaries and skipping temp identifiers. An initial broader version caused a -11 regression (false-positiving on destructured function params); the final version is scoped to non-temp identifiers and respects declaration boundaries (+1). Doc comments were added for the earlier `check_nested_method_call_as_argument`.

Second, `validate_no_ref_access_in_render.rs` gained a check in Pass 2 for `CallExpression` where a ref identifier is passed as an argument to a non-hook function (e.g., `renderApp(ref)`). This is distinct from the existing check that catches `ref.current` access — it catches the case where the ref object itself escapes into a call that is not a hook. The check inspects each argument of a `CallExpression`, and if any argument is a `LoadLocal` of a tracked ref identifier and the callee is not a hook, bails with a ref-access-in-render error (+1). Third, `program.rs` gained `is_valid_js_identifier` — a helper that validates `'use memo if(cond)'` directive conditions against JS identifier rules (must start with a Unicode letter/`_`/`$`, subsequent chars may be alphanumeric/`_`/`$`, must not be a JS reserved keyword like `true`/`false`/`null`). When the directive condition fails this check, compilation now bails with `InvalidDirective` instead of attempting to lower the invalid condition. This fixes two dynamic-gating fixtures where `cond` was a keyword (+2). The `known-failures.txt` was updated to remove all six newly passing fixtures.

| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_ref_access_in_render.rs` | Pass 2 `CallExpression` arg check: ref identifier passed to non-hook function |

## Phase 157: Stage 4e error.* fixtures — setState indirect, nested MethodCall, nested destructuring (+4, 495→499/1717)

**Date:** 2026-03-26
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 4e (error.* fixtures); .todo/bail-out-investigation.md -- Stage 2d (frozen-mutation blocker)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateNoSetStateInRender.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Codegen/CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/HIR/BuildHIR.ts`

Deep-work session targeting `error.*` conformance fixtures. Four distinct changes were shipped across the validation and HIR build layers.

First, `validate_no_set_state_in_render.rs` gained two new capabilities for indirect setState detection in `useMemo` callbacks. A new Pass 1.75 checks useMemo callbacks for transitive setState calls: when `useMemo(() => { fn() })` is encountered and `fn` was previously captured via `useCallback(() => { setState(x) })`, the validator now marks the memo callback as a setState-during-render violation. A supporting `check_nested_calls_set_state_transitively` helper performs the transitive walk. Additionally, when a `FunctionExpression` that calls setState is passed as a CallExpression argument (e.g., `useCallback(callback)`), the call's return value lvalue is also flagged as "calls setState", propagating the taint forward. The diagnostic message was extracted into a `SET_STATE_IN_RENDER_ERROR` constant to avoid duplication. This fixes `error.invalid-setState-in-useMemo-indirect-useCallback.js` (+1).

Second, `validate_no_unsupported_nodes.rs` gained `check_nested_method_call_as_argument`, a two-pass check that detects when a MethodCall result is used as an argument to another MethodCall (e.g., `Math.max(2, items.push(5))` or `Math.floor(diff.bar())`). The upstream compiler panics at codegen with "MethodCall::property must be an unpromoted + unmemoized MemberExpression" when this pattern occurs. The first pass collects all MethodCall lvalue IDs; the second pass checks whether any MethodCall argument references one of those IDs. This fixes `error.bug-invariant-codegen-methodcall.js` and `error.todo-nested-method-calls-lower-property-load-into-temporary.js` (+2).

Third, `build.rs` gained `has_nested_destructuring_target`, which detects nested destructuring in assignment expressions (e.g., `[[x]] = makeObject()`). When detected, it emits `UnsupportedNode("NestedDestructuringAssignment")`, which is caught by `validate_no_unsupported_nodes` via the `REJECTED_UNSUPPORTED_NODES` list and triggers a bail. This fixes `error.call-args-destructuring-asignment-complex.js` (+1).

Additionally, the Stage 2d frozen-mutation blocker was formally documented. The IIFE detection improvement in `validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` from Phase 156 was retained (two-pass per-block scheme) but confirmed as insufficient for the 15 remaining false positives. Root cause is transitive `MaybeFrozen` propagation in `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` via `PropertyStore`/`Capture` effects — the aliasing lattice needs a more precise representation to distinguish "receiver is frozen" from "a property of receiver holds a frozen value." Documented as a Stage 2d blocker in `.todo/bail-out-investigation.md`.

| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_unsupported_nodes.rs` | `check_nested_method_call_as_argument` two-pass MethodCall nesting check, added to `REJECTED_UNSUPPORTED_NODES` dispatch |

## Phase 156: Stage 2d — Frozen-Mutation False-Positive Investigation (495→495/1717, blocker)

**Date:** 2026-03-26
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 2d (fix frozen-mutation false-positive bails); .todo/bail-out-investigation.md -- Stage 2d
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateNoFreezingKnownMutableRanges.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts`

Deep-work session targeting Stage 2d: 26 fixtures where we bail with a frozen-mutation error but upstream compiles successfully. Three approaches were tried sequentially. Approach 1 (safe, no-op): improved IIFE detection in `validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` from a single-pass heuristic to a two-pass per-block scheme — first pass collects all IIFE callee identifiers within a block, second pass marks any `MutateFrozen` on those identifiers as exempt. This is structurally sound but irrelevant to the 26 failing fixtures because the false-positive `MutateFrozen` effect is placed on `mutate(y)`, not on the IIFE call site itself. Approach 2 (safe, no-op): attempted to skip Check 1 for `MutateFrozen` effects whose target is an IIFE call expression — same outcome, wrong location for the effect. Approach 3 (reverted): cross-referenced `MutateFrozen` effects against the `frozen_ids`/`frozen_names` sets in the validator to filter effects on variables that were never explicitly frozen in the current function scope. This caused a -2 regression (losing 2 true positives), because some frozen variables are captured indirectly and do appear in `frozen_ids` by the time the check fires. Reverted cleanly.

Root cause identified but not fixed: all 26 false positives originate in `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs`. The aliasing pass's `mutate()` method (line 225) propagates `MaybeFrozen` transitively through capture chains — when a mutable container `y` receives a property store `y.x = x` where `x` is (or contains) frozen params, `y` itself is marked `MaybeFrozen`. Any subsequent `mutate(y)` call then generates a `MutateFrozen` effect even though `y` itself was never frozen, only one of its properties. The correct fix is in the aliasing pass: `PropertyStore` and `Capture` effects should not unconditionally elevate the receiver to `MaybeFrozen` when only the stored value is frozen — the aliasing lattice needs a more precise representation (e.g., `FrozenProperty` distinct from `MaybeFrozen`). This is architecturally significant and carries high regression risk. The IIFE detection improvement and the conformance test reporting additions were retained as safe partial work.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` | Two-pass IIFE detection: first pass collects IIFE callee IDs per block, second pass exempts MutateFrozen on those IDs |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/conformance_tests.rs` | Added reporting sections for frozen-mutation bails, preserve-memo, silent bail-outs, both-no-memo, and slots-match categories |

---

## Phase 155: Fix preserve-memo dep validation (is_temp_name skip removal + HIR map pre-compute) (+31, 464→495/1717)

**Date:** 2026-03-26
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 4b (preserve-memo validation improvements)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidatePreservedManualMemoization.ts`

Three coordinated fixes to `validate_preserved_manual_memoization`. The first problem was that scope dep identifiers in the reactive function are SSA temps — they originate from call expressions, JSX, or other rvalues, not from `LoadLocal` lvalues. The existing code tried to resolve these temps by scanning `LoadLocal` instructions in the HIR, but by the time validation runs, `inline_load_locals` had already eliminated all `LoadLocal` instructions. The fix is to pre-compute a `HashMap<IdentifierId, Atom>` (temp id → source name) from the HIR before `build_reactive_function` consumes it. This map is threaded through the pipeline via `build_reactive_function`'s return value and forwarded to the validator.

The second problem was the `is_temp_name` skip: when a scope dep resolved to a temp name (i.e., was unresolvable), the validation logic silently skipped the comparison rather than treating the dep as a mismatch. Because every scope dep in the reactive function is an SSA temp, this skip suppressed ALL dep mismatch errors. The fix removes the skip and instead uses the pre-computed map to resolve temps to named locals; if still unresolvable, the dep is treated as a legitimate mismatch. The third fix corrects `compare_deps`: when the inferred dep is less specific than the source dep (e.g., inferred `propA` vs. source `propA.x`), the function was returning `Ok` (exact match); it now correctly returns `Subpath` (inferred is a subpath of the source), which triggers the appropriate mismatch diagnostic. The combined fixes pass all 18 preserve-memo error fixtures and 13 additional error fixtures for a net gain of +31 (464→495).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_preserved_manual_memoization.rs` | Remove `is_temp_name` skip, fix `compare_deps` Subpath return, use pre-computed HIR temp map for dep resolution |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Pre-compute HIR temp resolution map before `build_reactive_function` consumes the HIR; thread it to the validator |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 31 newly passing fixtures |

## Phase 154: Stage 3a2 — Zero-Slot Surplus Investigation (464→464/1717, no code change)

**Date:** 2026-03-26
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Stage 3a2 (zero-slot surplus investigation)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PruneNonEscapingScopes.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PruneUnusedScopes.ts`

Deep-work session investigating why 134+ fixtures emit zero-slot reactive scopes in our output where upstream emits none. Three concrete approaches were attempted; all were reverted. Approach 1: a per-function `function_has_any_reactive` pre-check guard was added to scope creation in `infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs` — if the function contains no reactive instructions at all, no scopes are created. This caused a -44 regression (464→420) because it suppressed scopes in functions that do have reactive content but were being incorrectly classified. Reverted. Approach 2: the `is_allocating` guard was removed from the `prune_unused_scopes` pass, allowing non-allocating scopes to be pruned rather than kept. This yielded a +3 gain but introduced an unresolved-reference bug (variable `setActive` became unresolvable in affected fixtures). Reverted. Approach 3: `prune_non_escaping_scopes` was audited in detail — confirmed it correctly retains scopes whose output escapes into JSX, callbacks, or return positions; the pruning logic is not the source of surplus scopes.

Root cause confirmed: the surplus is a scope inference problem (the same class of issue identified in Stage 3b). The `last_use_map` extension in `infer_reactive_scope_variables` assigns wider liveness ranges than upstream, causing adjacent scopes to be union-found into a single merged scope that spans hook calls. This merged scope is then assigned zero slots because it crosses an async boundary. The problem cannot be fixed by adjusting the pruning passes — it requires upstream-faithful liveness range computation in `infer_reactive_scope_variables`, which is the Stage 3b work item. The session also fixed two pre-existing snapshot test failures (codegen_validation_tests__semantic_conditional_component and per_pass_snapshots__hook_dependencies) that were generating noise in test output.

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/optimization/constant_propagation.rs` | Snapshot-only: snapshot rebaseline from prior dead branch elimination commit |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/optimization/dead_code_elimination.rs` | Snapshot-only: same rebaseline |
| `tests/snapshots/codegen_validation_tests__semantic_conditional_component.snap` | Fix pre-existing snapshot mismatch |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__hook_dependencies.snap` | Fix pre-existing snapshot mismatch |
