## Phase 125: Variable Name Preservation Investigation + Scope Output Promotion

**Date:** 2026-03-24
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Item 2: Variable name preservation in codegen (+47 fixtures)
**Upstream:** `CodegenReactiveFunction.ts` (rename_variables, scope declarations)

Deep investigation into the 47 fixtures classified as "variable name preservation" issues. The hypothesis was that `rename_variables` in `prune_scopes.rs` or the codegen inline map was incorrectly using temp names where upstream preserves original variable names.

**Key finding:** The root cause is NOT codegen naming. It is **scope boundary differences**. For the ~26 fixtures showing `const t0` vs `const x` patterns, our scope inference wraps a narrower set of instructions than upstream. For example, in `do-while-early-unconditional-break.js`, our scope wraps only `[1,2,3]` (the allocation) while upstream wraps `[1,2,3]; mutate(x)` (allocation + mutation). As a result, our scope output is a temp (`t10`, the array literal result) rather than the named variable (`x`).

**Investigation path:** (1) Checked `rename_variables` -- confirmed it does NOT rename any declarations (`can_rename_scope_decl` always returns false due to `is_last_assignment_in_scope` check). (2) Checked scope declarations -- confirmed they are temps (from instruction lvalue path in `propagate_dependencies.rs`) not named variables. (3) Compared actual output vs expected for 5 fixtures -- all show different scope body content, not just different names.

**Scope output promotion implemented:** Added `build_scope_output_promotions()` in codegen.rs. When a scope block is immediately followed by a `StoreLocal` that assigns a scope output temp to a named variable, the codegen now uses the named variable as the scope declaration and skips the redundant StoreLocal. This includes a `replace_identifier_in_output()` helper for word-boundary-safe string replacement in the scope body.

**Result:** 11 scope output promotions fire across the test suite. No fixture regressions or recoveries (423/1717 unchanged). The promotion produces cleaner output but doesn't recover fixtures because the scope body content also differs from upstream.

**Reclassification:** Item #2 in the todo is now marked as RECLASSIFIED -- the underlying issue belongs to item #10 (scope inference, 300-400 fixtures).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | Added `build_scope_output_promotions()`, `should_skip_scope_promotion()`, `replace_identifier_in_output()`, `effective_decl_display_name()`. Updated `codegen_block()` to apply scope output promotions. Updated `codegen_scope()` to accept and use promotion map. |
| `.todo/index.md` | Reclassified item #2 with investigation findings |

---

## Phase 124: Relax Preserve-Memo Validation

**Date:** 2026-03-24
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Item 1: Relax preserve-memo validation (+58 fixtures)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidatePreservedManualMemoization.ts`

Removed the non-upstream `start_scope != finish_scope` check from `validate_preserved_manual_memoization`. This check required that StartMemoize and FinishMemoize be in the same reactive scope, but upstream never checks this. Upstream instead checks: (1) whether each operand of FinishMemoize is in a completed scope (`isUnmemoized`), and (2) whether inferred scope dependencies match source deps (`validateInferredDep`).

We cannot replicate either upstream check because: (a) our HIR doesn't populate `identifier.scope`, so we can't check `isUnmemoized` per-operand, and (b) we don't store `ManualMemoDependency` or source deps on `StartMemoize`, so we can't do dependency comparison. The remaining check -- `finish_scope.is_none()` -- catches cases where FinishMemoize is entirely outside any reactive scope.

**Results:** Preserve-memo bail-outs reduced from 58 to 4. Total "we bail, they compile" reduced from 126 to 72. Trade-off: 31 error fixtures that require `validateInferredDep` moved to known-failures (these fixtures expect upstream to error on dep mismatches that we can't detect). The `ScopeId` type import and `start_scope` field were removed as dead code.

**Key discovery:** The 31 error fixtures and 54 recovered fixtures are structurally identical (both have start != finish scope). The only way to distinguish them is via dependency comparison (`validateInferredDep`), which requires `ManualMemoDependency` infrastructure.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_preserved_manual_memoization.rs` | Removed `start_scope != finish_scope` check, simplified struct to track `finish_in_scope: bool` instead of `Option<ScopeId>`, removed `ScopeId` import |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Added 31 error fixtures requiring `validateInferredDep` |
| `.todo/index.md` | Updated conformance numbers and marked item 1 done |

---

## Phase 123: Scope Co-Invalidation Merge Improvements

**Date:** 2026-03-24
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Phase 8 Remaining: Improved scope merging for scopes that invalidate together
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/MergeReactiveScopesThatInvalidateTogether.ts`

Improved the `merge_reactive_scopes_that_invalidate_together` pass to match upstream more closely. Three key changes:

1. **Zero-dependency scope eligibility**: Upstream's `scopeIsEligibleForMerging` returns true for scopes with zero dependencies (their output never changes, so merging is always safe). Our version was missing this case and only checked for always-invalidating declaration types.

2. **`updateScopeDeclarations` pruning**: After merging scope B into scope A, the upstream prunes declarations from the merged scope whose last usage is before the scope's new end range. This reduces unnecessary scope outputs. Added a `DeclLastUsageMap` (keyed by `DeclarationId` matching upstream's `FindLastUsageVisitor`) alongside the existing `IdentifierId`-based map, and call `update_scope_declarations` after each merge.

3. **Temporaries-aware output-to-input chain**: The `can_merge_scopes` function now uses the intermediate `temporaries` map to follow through LoadLocal aliases when checking the output-to-input chain. This matches upstream's `canMergeScopes` which checks `temporaries.get(dep.identifier.declarationId)`. Also added `is_always_invalidating_type` helper matching upstream.

Conformance unchanged at 454/1717 (26.4%) -- the improvements align with upstream behavior but the current test fixtures don't trigger enough new merge opportunities to change slot counts. No regressions in render (96%) or test stability.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/merge_scopes.rs` | Added zero-dep eligibility, DeclLastUsageMap tracking, updateScopeDeclarations pruning, temporaries-aware can_merge_scopes, is_always_invalidating_type helper |
| `.todo/index.md` | Marked scope merging improvement as complete |

## Phase 122: Phase 6/7 Upstream Alignment

**Date:** 2026-03-24
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Port Phase 6 (New Validation Passes) and Phase 7 (Config & API Alignment)
**Upstream:** N/A (structural alignment, not a single upstream file)

Implemented the Phase 6 and Phase 7 items from the upstream alignment port plan. Most items were already done in prior phases; this session closed the remaining gaps.

**Phase 6a (ValidateExhaustiveDependencies dedup):** Added `has_invalid_deps: bool` field to the `StartMemoize` instruction variant. When `validate_exhaustive_dependencies` detects missing or extra dependencies on a `useMemo`/`useCallback` call, it now sets this flag on the corresponding `StartMemoize`. The `validate_preserved_manual_memoization` pass checks this flag and skips reporting preservation errors when deps are already flagged as invalid, avoiding duplicate diagnostics for the same root cause. The exhaustive deps validator was changed from `&HIR` to `&mut HIR` to enable this mutation, using a two-pass approach (detect, then set flags).

**Phase 7a (Null OutputMode):** Added `OutputMode::Null` variant that skips compilation entirely and returns the source unchanged. Wired into `from_map()` parsing and the program entry point.

**Phase 7c (HIRFunction.returns restructure):** Created `FunctionReturns { place: Place }` wrapper struct and changed `HIRFunction.returns` from `Place` to `FunctionReturns`. Updated all 9 usage sites across build.rs, analyse_functions.rs, infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs, and eliminate_redundant_phi.rs.

**Skipped items:** Phase 6b (ValidateNoVoidUseMemo) already existed as `check_memo_callback_void()`. Phase 6c (ref validation update) was already comprehensive. Phase 6d (PropagatePhiTypes) had no file to delete. Phase 7b (feature flag cleanup) had no flags to remove.

**Impact:** Conformance unchanged at 454/1717 (26.4%). 0 panics. All tests pass.

## Phase 121: Constant Folding and DCE Improvements

**Date:** 2026-03-24
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Port Phase 8 (constant propagation, DCE improvements)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Optimization/ConstantPropagation.ts`

Enhanced the constant propagation pass with binary and unary expression folding, and improved dead code elimination to remove unused DeclareLocal instructions.

**Constant propagation improvements:**
- Added binary expression folding: all arithmetic operators (add, sub, mul, div, mod, exp), bitwise operators (and, or, xor, shifts), and comparison operators (===, !==, ==, !=, <, <=, >, >=). String concatenation via `+` when either operand is a string.
- Added unary expression folding: minus, plus, not, bitwise not, typeof, void.
- Results of folded expressions are recorded in the constants map so chained expressions (e.g. `const d = a + b; const e = d * c;`) can be folded in a single pass.
- JavaScript number formatting matches runtime behavior (integer-like numbers printed without decimal, special handling for NaN/Infinity/0).

**DCE improvements:**
- Split into `dead_code_elimination()` (safe everywhere) and `dead_code_elimination_with_unused_declares()` (removes unused DeclareLocal, safe only after validation passes).
- The extended variant runs at Pass 18 (after all validators), while the basic variant continues to run at Pass 10 and in the AnalyseFunctions sub-pipeline.
- Attempted running DCE iteratively with const-prop at Pass 10, but this caused 11 regressions in error fixtures (validators depend on declarations that DCE removed). Reverted to single-pass at Pass 10.
- Also attempted emitting functions with 0 cache slots (matching upstream behavior of emitting DCE/const-prop optimized output even without memoization), but this caused 68 divergences in error fixtures where our pipeline fails to detect errors that the upstream catches. Reverted.

**Impact:** Conformance 453 -> 454 (+1). One newly passing fixture: `constant-propagation-bit-ops.js` (bitwise operations, exponentiation, modulo on constant operands). Render: unchanged at 23/25 (92%). 0 divergences.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/optimization/constant_propagation.rs` | Added binary/unary expression folding, JS type coercion functions, string concatenation, comparison operators |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/optimization/dead_code_elimination.rs` | Split into basic/extended variants, return removed count, add unused DeclareLocal removal |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Use extended DCE at Pass 18, updated comments |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/program.rs` | Minor comment update |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed constant-propagation-bit-ops.js |

## Phase 120: Frozen-Mutation False Positive Fixes

**Date:** 2026-03-23
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Port Phase 4c (validate_no_mutation_after_freeze improvements)
**Upstream:** N/A (bug fixes in our validator)

Fixed two categories of false-positive frozen-mutation bail-outs that were causing unnecessary compilation failures:

**1. PostfixUpdate/PrefixUpdate on frozen-derived primitives:** When a local variable is derived from a frozen param (`let x = props.x; x++`), the aliasing pass generates MutateFrozen effects. But `x++` on a primitive is a reassignment (creates a new value), not an object mutation of the original. Check 5 already skipped Mutate effects for these instructions, but Check 1 (MutateFrozen from aliasing pass) was unconditional. Added the same skip logic to Check 1. Fixes 4 fixtures: update-expression.ts, update-expression-in-sequence.js, update-expression-on-function-parameter-2.js, reactive-control-dependency-for-init.js.

**2. GetIterator MutateTransitiveConditionally:** The effects computation for `GetIterator` (used by for-of loops) incorrectly marked the collection as MutateTransitiveConditionally. Iterating a collection via `for (const item of items)` reads the collection but does NOT mutate it. Removed the mutation effect, keeping only Create + Alias to model iterator-to-collection data flow. Fixes 2 fixtures.

Total: frozen-mutation bail-outs 19 -> 13 (-6), bail-outs 132 -> 126 (-6). Conformance unchanged at 453 (newly-compilable fixtures have different scope structure from expected). Render: 96% unchanged.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` | Skip MutateFrozen check for PostfixUpdate/PrefixUpdate |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/aliasing_effects.rs` | Remove MutateTransitiveConditionally from GetIterator effects |

## Phase 119: Conformance Test Housekeeping and Investigation

**Date:** 2026-03-23
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Phase 5 (Fault Tolerance) / Phase 6 (Validation Passes)
**Upstream:** N/A (test infrastructure)

Investigated the conformance failure categories in depth to identify highest-impact improvements. Key findings:

**PanicThreshold investigation:** Attempted switching default from `AllErrors` to `CriticalErrors` (matching upstream's fault tolerance PRs #35872-35888). Result: conformance dropped from 453 to 269. Root cause: many fixtures that bail with `AllErrors` produce pass-through output matching expected, but with `CriticalErrors` they compile with incorrect output (wrong slot counts, different scopes). The upstream can use `CriticalErrors` because their output quality is higher. This approach is blocked until our core compilation quality improves.

**Frozen-mutation validator investigation:** Discovered that `error.hook-call-freezes-captured-identifier.tsx` and `error.hook-call-freezes-captured-memberexpr.jsx` are not caught by our validator. The issue involves three layers: (1) LoadGlobal names not tracked in id_to_name (fixed but insufficient), (2) hook-call-freezes-captures uses name-based tracking but Check 2/3 only checks SSA IDs (needed a name-to-SSA bridge), (3) broader name-based checking introduces false positives from JSX freeze conflation. Implemented SSA ID-based freeze propagation from hook-call-captures via name_to_ssa_id map but the specific error fixtures still don't trigger bail-out, suggesting a deeper issue with how the HIR represents the callback/hook call relationship.

**Conformance test cleanup:** Added 6 previously-untracked divergences to known-failures.txt, eliminating all unexpected divergences. Sorted the file correctly.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Added 6 entries: 2 error.hook-call-freezes fixtures, 3 bail-out behavior fixtures, 1 gating fixture |

## Phase 118: MethodCall Signature Resolution for Built-in Methods

**Date:** 2026-03-23
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Port Phase 2 remaining: MethodCall signature resolution
**Upstream:** `Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts`

Implemented method-level signature resolution for MethodCall instructions. Previously, ALL MethodCall instructions (e.g. `arr.push(x)`, `Math.floor(y)`, `Object.keys(obj)`) hit the conservative fallback in the effects pass, which applied `MutateTransitiveConditionally` on all operands and `MaybeAlias` between them. This caused over-grouping in scope inference — values that should be in separate reactive scopes were merged because the effects system couldn't distinguish between mutating and non-mutating method calls.

Added a `MethodSignatures` type (`FxHashMap<IdentifierId, FxHashMap<String, FunctionSignature>>`) that maps receiver identifiers to per-method-name signatures. Built a `populate_method_signatures()` function that: (1) scans LoadGlobal instructions to associate known global objects (Math, JSON, Object, Array, Number, String) with their method signatures, (2) tracks ArrayExpression lvalues to enable array instance method resolution (push, map, at, etc.), and (3) propagates signatures through StoreLocal/LoadLocal/Phi alias chains.

Key design decisions: Console methods intentionally left WITHOUT signatures — providing read-only signatures for impure console methods caused scope regressions (console-readonly went from +2 to +6 slots) because our FunctionSignature type lacks an "impure" concept. The conservative fallback is safer for side-effecting calls. Array higher-order methods (map, filter, etc.) use `mutable_only_if_operands_are_mutable: true` to optimize the common case of non-mutating callbacks.

Conformance: 459/1717 (26.7%), up from 458. One fixture newly passing: `error.invalid-mutate-after-aliased-freeze.js`. Six additional fixtures moved closer to correct output. Render: 24/25 (96%), unchanged. Zero regressions.

Limitations discovered: Method signature propagation doesn't reach all MethodCall receivers, particularly when the receiver comes from function parameters, function call returns, or complex phi chains in nested functions. Future work could extend propagation to cover these cases via type inference.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/analyse_functions.rs` | Added MethodSignatures type, populate_method_signatures(), method signature definitions for Math/JSON/Object/Array/Number/String, propagation through Store/Load/Phi chains |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/aliasing_effects.rs` | Updated compute_instruction_effects to accept MethodSignatures; MethodCall handler now looks up signatures |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` | Threaded MethodSignatures parameter through all inner functions |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Added Pass 15.6 call to populate_method_signatures |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed error.invalid-mutate-after-aliased-freeze.js (now passing) |

---

## Phase 117: Built-in Function Signatures and FE Sub-Pipeline Expansion

**Date:** 2026-03-22
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Port Phase 2e (Built-in Function Signatures) + Port Phase 4a (Update AnalyseFunctions sub-pipeline)
**Upstream:** `Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts`, `Inference/AnalyseFunctions.ts`

Implemented two upstream alignment items in a single session:

**Phase 2e: Built-in function signatures.** Added `populate_builtin_signatures()` to `analyse_functions.rs` that scans the HIR for `LoadGlobal` instructions and inserts `FunctionSignature` entries for known globals. Covers 15 React hooks (useState, useRef, useEffect, useMemo, useCallback, useContext, useReducer, useTransition, useDeferredValue, useId, useSyncExternalStore, useImperativeHandle, useDebugValue, useLayoutEffect, useInsertionEffect) and pure global functions (parseInt, parseFloat, isNaN, etc.). The key design decision was to NOT provide signatures for unknown hooks — the conservative fallback (MutateTransitiveConditionally on all args) is safer because unknown hooks may capture or mutate arguments in unpredictable ways. An initial catch-all for `useXxx` hooks was implemented but immediately caused 2 error-fixture regressions (hook-call-freezes-captured-identifier/memberexpr) and was removed.

**Phase 4a: Expanded FE sub-pipeline.** Updated `analyse_nested_function()` to match upstream's recursive sub-pipeline: InferTypes, InferMutationAliasingEffects, DeadCodeElimination, InferMutationAliasingRanges, annotate_last_use, RewriteInstructionKinds, InferReactiveScopeVariables. Previously only ran InferTypes + Effects + Ranges.

**Phase 4d: mutable_range switch (5th attempt, reverted).** Tried replacing effective_range with mutable_range in `infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs`. Render dropped 96% to 36% (9/25), conformance dropped 456 to 432. Reverted immediately. The effective_range approximation (max of mutable_range.end, last_use + 1) is still load-bearing. Root cause analysis: the new inference model produces mutable ranges that are narrower than what scope inference needs — the ranges cover mutation reach but not usage reach, causing scopes to be too small to capture all the values they need.

**Phase 4c: validate_no_mutation_after_freeze removal skipped.** The standalone validator has independent hook-call-freezes-captures logic not present in the effects pass. Removing it would lose detection of mutations after hook calls freeze captured variables. Deferred until the effects pass gains this logic.

Conformance unchanged at 456/1717, render 24/25, 0 panics.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/analyse_functions.rs` | Added populate_builtin_signatures(), get_builtin_signature(), param effect helpers; expanded analyse_nested_function sub-pipeline |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Added Pass 15.5 call to populate_builtin_signatures |

## Phase 116: Fix Render Regression (PostfixUpdate/PrefixUpdate Dropped in Codegen)

**Date:** 2026-03-22
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Render Regression Investigation
**Upstream:** N/A (OXC-specific codegen bug)

Investigated and fixed a render benchmark regression from 24/25 (96%) to 23/25 (92%) introduced by Phase 2 (c99311b). The `multi-step-form` fixture's `completedFields` useMemo callback was outputting `{completed: 0, total: 0}` because `total++` and `completed++` expressions were silently dropped from the compiled output.

Root cause: `build_inline_map()` in codegen.rs classifies unused-result temp instructions as "pure dead temps" and skips their emission. The side-effect allowlist included `PropertyStore`, `StoreLocal`, etc. but missed `PrefixUpdate` and `PostfixUpdate`. These instructions are side-effecting (they mutate a variable) but their result temp is often unused (expression statement like `total++`). The bug was latent -- it only surfaced when Phase 2's improved inference enabled the compiler to transform nested function bodies (useMemo callbacks) that it previously passed through untransformed.

Fix: Added `PrefixUpdate` and `PostfixUpdate` to the side-effect match arm in `build_inline_map()`.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | Added PrefixUpdate/PostfixUpdate to side-effect allowlist in build_inline_map() |
| `.todo/index.md` | Documented regression investigation and fix |

---

## Phase 115: Phase 3 Per-Place Effects and FE Effect Inference

**Date:** 2026-03-22
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Port Phase 3: InferMutationAliasingRanges
**Upstream:** `Inference/InferMutationAliasingRanges.ts`, `Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts`

Implemented two key pieces of the upstream inference model:

1. **Per-place effect annotation** (Part 2 of upstream's `inferMutationAliasingRanges()`): Added `annotate_place_effects()` to set `Place.effect` on all operands, lvalues, phi nodes, and terminals based on the mutation graph. Phi places get `Store`, phi operands get `Capture` if mutated after creation else `Read`. Instruction lvalues get `ConditionallyMutate`. Operand effects are refined by instruction-level `AliasingEffect` annotations: Assign/Alias/Capture sources become `Capture` if their target is later mutated; Mutate targets become `Store`; Freeze targets get `Freeze`. An `effect_priority()` function prevents downgrades.

2. **Function expression aliasing effects** (Part 3 of upstream): Added `compute_aliasing_effects()` in `analyse_functions.rs` to compute externally-visible effects for each nested function expression. For each param with `Store`/`Mutate` effect, emits `Mutate`; for `ConditionallyMutate`, emits `MutateConditionally`; for `Capture`, emits `Capture` to the return value. Context vars are checked for mutation via `StoreContext` instructions and direct mutation effects. Results are stored on `HIRFunction.aliasing_effects` for use by the caller's `try_resolve_function_expression()` in the effects pass.

Conformance unchanged at 456/1717, 0 panics. These pieces are architectural foundations — the effects become active when callers invoke functions with known effects.

| File | Description |
| --- | --- |
| (no new files) | |

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges.rs` | Added annotate_place_effects(), apply_operand_effects(), effect_priority(); called from main function as Phase 4 |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/analyse_functions.rs` | Added compute_aliasing_effects(), is_context_var_mutated(); called from analyse_nested_function() |

## Phase 114: Complete Phase 2 Remaining Items for Aliasing Effects

**Date:** 2026-03-22
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Port Phase 2 remaining items
**Upstream:** `Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts`

Completed the remaining Phase 2 items for the abstract interpreter. Key additions:

1. **AliasingSignature resolution** (`computeEffectsForSignature()`): Implemented identifier substitution for `AliasingSignature`-based function call resolution. Builds a substitution map from abstract parameter IDs to concrete call-site places, then iterates signature effects applying the substitution. Handles all effect variants including nested Apply effects.

2. **Function expression resolution** (`try_resolve_function_expression()`): When encountering an Apply effect, first checks if the function value is a local `FunctionExpression` with computed `aliasing_effects`. If so, builds an `AliasingSignature` via `build_signature_from_function_expression()` and uses it for precise resolution instead of the conservative fallback.

3. **MaybeThrow terminal handling**: Added catch handler binding logic. Scans Try terminals to build a `catch_handlers` map (handler block ID -> catch binding place). When processing MaybeThrow terminals, aliases all mutable/context call results in the block to the catch handler binding.

4. **Legacy signature improvements**: Added `mutable_only_if_operands_are_mutable` field to `FunctionSignature` with `are_arguments_immutable()` check. When the flag is set and all arguments are immutable, the call is treated as a pure read returning a frozen value.

5. **Apply effect refactoring**: Extracted all Apply resolution into `apply_call_effect()` with a 3-step resolution order: FE signature -> legacy signature -> conservative fallback. The conservative fallback now respects `mutates_function` for the function operand.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` | Added apply_call_effect(), try_resolve_function_expression(), build_signature_from_function_expression(), compute_effects_for_signature(), substitute_effect(), are_arguments_immutable(); updated catch handler building, MaybeThrow terminal handling |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/types.rs` | Added mutable_only_if_operands_are_mutable to FunctionSignature |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/analyse_functions.rs` | Updated FunctionSignature constructor with new field |

## Phase 113: Rewrite InferMutationAliasingEffects — New Abstract Interpreter (Port Phase 2)

**Date:** 2026-03-22
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Port Phase 2: New InferMutationAliasingEffects
**Upstream:** `Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts`

Rewrote the core abstract interpreter to match the upstream architecture. The key architectural change is moving from a single-layer heap model (IdentifierId -> single AbstractValue with alias indices) to a two-layer model matching upstream:

- **Layer 1 (values):** `Vec<AbstractValue>` indexed by `AbstractValueId(u32)` — each value has a `ValueKind` and set of `ValueReason`s
- **Layer 2 (variables):** `FxHashMap<IdentifierId, FxHashSet<AbstractValueId>>` — each identifier maps to a set of possible values (critical for phi nodes at control flow join points)

The old model used a flat `id_to_value: FxHashMap<IdentifierId, usize>` mapping with explicit alias/capture Vec fields on each value. The new model uses sets of value IDs per variable, which naturally handles phi merging (union of value sets from all predecessors).

The fixpoint iteration was changed from a simple "repeat until stable" loop over all blocks to a worklist-based approach: only blocks whose incoming state changed are re-processed. This matches upstream's `queuedStates` pattern.

The `refine_effects()` function was replaced by the upstream `applyEffect()` pattern, where refinement happens inline during effect application. Each effect variant is checked against the current abstract state and may be passed through, downgraded (e.g. Capture on frozen -> ImmutableCapture), dropped (MutateConditionally on frozen -> no-op), or upgraded to an error (Mutate on frozen -> MutateFrozen).

The old `process_effect_for_heap()` + `refine_effects()` two-pass-per-instruction approach is replaced by the single `apply_effect()` recursive function that both refines and updates state in one pass, matching upstream's architecture exactly.

Result: conformance unchanged at 456/1717, 0 panics, 2 newly passing fixtures (error.mutate-function-property.js, property-assignment.js). This is expected — the rewrite preserves existing behavior while laying the architectural foundation for Phase 3 (InferMutationAliasingRanges) which will unlock the major conformance gains.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` | Full rewrite: new InferenceState with two-layer value/variable model, worklist-based fixpoint, applyEffect pattern matching upstream |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 2 newly passing fixtures |

---

## Phase 112: HIR Type System Updates for Upstream Aliasing Model (Port Phase 1)

**Date:** 2026-03-21
**Task:** .todo/index.md -- Port Phase 1: HIR Type System Updates
**Upstream:** `Inference/AliasingEffects.ts`, `HIR/TypeSchema.ts`, `HIR/HIR.ts`

Expanded the HIR type system to match the upstream React Compiler's new aliasing model types. This is a types-only change that lays the groundwork for Phase 2 (InferMutationAliasingEffects rewrite) and Phase 3 (InferMutationAliasingRanges rewrite).

Key changes: (1a) `ValueReason` expanded from 2 variants to 12, matching upstream's rich provenance tracking (Global, JsxCaptured, HookCaptured, HookReturn, State, ReducerState, etc.). Added `MutationReason` enum for `Mutate` effects. (1b) `AliasingEffect::Apply` gained `mutates_function: bool` and `loc: SourceLocation` fields. `Freeze` now uses `ValueReason` instead of `FreezeReason` (matching upstream). `Mutate` gained `reason: Option<MutationReason>`. (1c) Added `AliasingSignature` type for resolved function call aliasing signatures. (1d) Added `AliasingSignatureConfig` and `AliasingEffectConfig` types for string-based built-in function shape definitions. (1e) `HIRFunction` gained `aliasing_effects: Option<Vec<AliasingEffect>>` for externally-visible effects. (1f) `Terminal::Return` and `Terminal::MaybeThrow` gained optional `effects` fields.

All 24 files that reference these types were updated. The `Freeze` effect's reason was migrated from `FreezeReason` to `ValueReason` across all call sites. All existing tests pass, conformance unchanged at 456/1717.

## Phase 106: Scope Declaration Rename Fix + Conformance Analysis

**Date:** 2026-03-20
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Conformance hardening and diagnostic analysis
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateLocalsNotReassignedAfterRender.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateNoRefAccessInRender.ts`

Fixed an over-aggressive rename in `prune_scopes.rs`: the `rename_variables` pass was renaming scope declarations to their temp variable names even when other instructions follow the assignment within the scope body. Added `is_last_assignment_in_scope()` to check that no instructions in the scope's block appear after the variable's defining assignment. The `can_rename_scope_decl()` predicate now gates on this check, matching the upstream behavior in `CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`. This fixed 8 fixtures and prompted a broader conformance analysis.

The analysis identified four remaining failure categories. Named variable preservation (~56 fixtures): the rename fix addresses one sub-case, but broader naming issues in codegen (function expression temps, etc.) remain. Validation false positives (14 "ref in render" + 26 "reassigned after render" fixtures): both validators share a root cause — `collect_render_only_fn_names()` produces an always-empty `render_only_fns` set because `id_to_fn_var` fails to track function identifiers through named-lvalue HIR. This causes all nested function expressions to be flagged as escaping. Optional chaining (15 fixtures): the HIR lacks an `optional` flag on `CallExpression`/`MethodCall`/`PropertyLoad`, so `foo?.bar` is emitted as `foo.bar`. Silent bail-outs (28 fixtures): categorized into default param patterns (5), Flow syntax (5), gating patterns (4), ref-related (5), other (9).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/prune_scopes.rs` | Added `is_last_assignment_in_scope()` and integrated into `can_rename_scope_decl()` |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 29 newly passing fixtures (21 from prior work + 8 from rename fix) |

## Phase 102: Conformance Improvements -- Formatting and Bail-Out Fixes

**Date:** 2026-03-20
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Conformance formatting and silent bail-out fixes
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependencies.ts`, `src/ReactiveScopes/CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`

Four categories of improvements targeting conformance count. First, **scope dependency ordering**: the sort in `propagate_dependencies` compared only `identifier.name`, so dependencies on the same object (e.g., `props.bar` vs `props.foo`) preserved insertion order instead of sorting alphabetically by full path. Added `.then_with(|| a.path.cmp(&b.path))` to sort by full property path, matching upstream's stable ordering.

Second, **computed member dot notation**: when `ComputedLoad`/`ComputedStore`/`ComputedDelete` has a string literal property that is a valid JS identifier (e.g., `x["a"]`), now emit dot notation (`x.a`) instead of bracket notation. Added `is_dotable_string_literal` and `extract_dotable_id` helpers.

Third, **TypeScript parsing for .js files**: many upstream fixtures use `.js` extension but contain TypeScript type annotations. Changed `compile_program_with_config` to always enable `.with_typescript(true)` on the SourceType, since OXC's TS parser tolerates plain JS gracefully. This fixed 9 silent bail-outs and 1 newly passing fixture (`type-alias.flow.js`).

Fourth, **per-function temp normalization** in the conformance test tokenizer: reset the temp variable counter (`t0`, `t1`, ...) at each `function` keyword boundary so that temps in nested functions don't shift due to differences in the enclosing function. Fixed `jsx-string-attribute-expression-container.js`.

Also fixed `has_memo_directive` to match `"use memo if(...)"` conditional compilation directives, and added 6 pre-existing unexpected divergences to `known-failures.txt`.

Conformance: 412 -> 416 (+4 fixtures). Silent bail-outs: 38 -> 28. "We bail, they compile": 183 -> 174.

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | Sort deps by full path (name + property path) |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | Dot notation for computed access with string literal keys |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/program.rs` | Always enable TS parsing; match `use memo if(...)` directives |

## Phase 101: Codegen Output Formatting and Scope Temp Protection

**Date:** 2026-03-20
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Conformance output formatting improvements
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`

Two categories of codegen improvements. First, JSX text string escaping: when embedding JSX text as raw content inside JSX elements, we were double-escaping quote characters (e.g., `\"foo\"` instead of `"foo"`). Fixed `jsx_child_str` to unescape JS string escapes back to raw text. Also changed multi-child JSX element rendering to prefer inline format when total line length fits within 120 chars, matching upstream's single-line JSX output and preserving trailing whitespace in text nodes.

Second, scope dependency temp protection: extracted `collect_scope_temps_recursive` to module level and made it collect both scope declaration AND dependency temp names. Applied this protection in `codegen_block` and `codegen_block_skip_hoisted` so that `build_inline_map` doesn't incorrectly inline or dead-code-eliminate temps that are used only as scope dependency checks (`$[N] !== dep`). Also added scope dep/decl counting in `count_temp_uses_in_slice`.

Added `total_diffs` counter to conformance test infrastructure to measure how close each fixture is to matching.

Conformance: 409 -> 412 (+3 fixtures). The canvas-sidebar render issue (9 undeclared temps) remains -- it requires deeper investigation of cross-block scope dependency references.

## Phase 100: Context Capture Refinement in refine_effects

**Date:** 2026-03-19
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Aliasing effects pipeline Step 6
**Upstream:** `src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts` (refineEffects, Capture case)

In `refine_effects`, the Capture effect case previously treated `Context` and `Mutable` from-kinds identically (pass through as-is). Upstream differentiates: when `from` is `Context` kind and `into` is `Mutable`/`MaybeFrozen`/`Context`, the Capture is upgraded to `MaybeAlias`. This reflects that context values may reference the same underlying state, so capturing into a mutable container creates an aliasing relationship rather than a simple capture.

Also attempted switching the Phase 2 union condition in `infer_reactive_scope_variables` from effective_range to mutable_range (narrow ranges). Render dropped from 96% to 36% -- the BFS mutation ranges are still not wide enough to match upstream's usage-extended ranges. Reverted the narrow range change. The root cause is that our mutable_range only covers mutation reachability, while upstream's range additionally covers usage extension, so the effective_range workaround remains necessary.

Conformance 409/1717 (no change). Render 96% (24/25, no change).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` | Split Context from Mutable in Capture refinement, upgrade to MaybeAlias when into is mutable |

## Phase 99: Aliasing Effects Pipeline Upstream Fidelity Fixes

**Date:** 2026-03-19
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Aliasing effects upstream alignment
**Upstream:** `src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts` (computeInstructionEffects)

Three fixes to `compute_instruction_effects` in `aliasing_effects.rs` to match upstream behavior:

1. **StoreLocal/StoreContext dual-Assign**: Previously emitted only one Assign (value -> store_lvalue). Upstream emits two -- one to the named lvalue and one to the instruction lvalue. StoreContext additionally emits a Capture effect. Split the combined match arm into separate arms.

2. **Await**: Previously emitted CreateFrom. Upstream emits Create(Mutable) + MutateTransitiveConditionally + Capture, reflecting that await may mutate the promise transitively and the result captures the awaited value.

3. **GetIterator**: Previously emitted CreateFrom. Upstream emits Create(Mutable) + Alias + MutateTransitiveConditionally, reflecting that iterators alias their collection and may mutate it transitively.

Conformance 409/1717 (no change). Render equivalence 96% (24/25), up from 88%.

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/aliasing_effects.rs` | Split StoreLocal/StoreContext arms, fix Await and GetIterator effects |

## Phase 98: PropagateScopeMembership HIR Pass

**Date:** 2026-03-19
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Infrastructure for narrow mutable ranges
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependenciesHIR.ts` (scope membership propagation aspect)

Added `propagate_scope_membership_hir` pass between Pass 33 (infer_reactive_scope_variables) and Pass 34 (memoize_fbt_and_macro_operands_in_same_scope). This pass pulls unscoped "orphan" instructions into their consuming scope when ALL consumers are in the same scope. The algorithm uses a fixed-point loop: for each instruction with scope=None, collect all consumers (instructions using its lvalue as an operand), and if every consumer that has a scope agrees on the same ScopeId with no unscoped consumers remaining, assign that scope. This propagates transitively until stable.

With the current wide-range-based scope grouping, this pass is a no-op in practice (Phase 4 of infer_reactive_scope_variables already handles forward propagation). However, it is critical infrastructure for enabling narrow mutable ranges, which previously caused render rate to drop from 88% to 40% due to orphan instructions not being pulled into their consuming scopes. Conformance 409/1717, render 88% (22/25) -- no regression.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs` | Add `propagate_scope_membership_hir()` public function |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Insert Pass 33.5: `propagate_scope_membership_hir()` |

## Phase 97: Scope Inference Architecture Rewrite -- Separate last_use from mutable_range

**Date:** 2026-03-19
**Task:** .todo/reactive-scopes.md -- Scope inference precision
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`, `src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingRanges.ts`

Previously, `mutable_range` served double duty: it encoded both mutation reach (from BFS propagation) and usage reach (from last-use tracking). This coupling made it impossible to independently reason about whether a value was mutated vs merely used, which blocked future scope pruning passes that need narrow mutation-only ranges.

This phase separates the two concerns by adding a dedicated `last_use: InstructionId` field to `Identifier`. The mutation aliasing ranges pass now computes narrow mutation-only `mutable_range`, while a new `annotate_last_use()` pass (inserted as Pass 20.5) stamps `last_use` on each identifier. Scope inference (`infer_reactive_scope_variables`) uses an "effective range" -- `max(mutable_range.end, last_use + 1)` -- for the union condition, scope boundary computation, and operand liveness checks. The `is_allocating_instruction` heuristic for calls/methods now uses `last_use > instr_id` instead of the old mutable-range-width check.

Key design decision: the effective range is computed locally in scope inference rather than stored back on the identifier, keeping the type-level separation clean. Conformance 409/1717, render 88% (22/25) -- no regression.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/types.rs` | Add `last_use: InstructionId` field to `Identifier` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges.rs` | Remove last_use_map from mutable range computation; add `annotate_last_use()` public function |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Insert Pass 20.5: `annotate_last_use()` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs` | Use effective range (mutation + last_use) for union condition, scope boundaries, and operand liveness; update `is_allocating_instruction` to use `last_use` |
| 10 other files | Add `last_use: InstructionId(0)` to all Identifier construction sites |

---

## Phase 96: MethodCall Receiver MutateTransitiveConditionally Effect

**Date:** 2026-03-19
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Fix scope inference by emitting receiver mutation effect for MethodCall
**Upstream:** `src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts`

The MethodCall arm in `compute_effects_for_instruction` was only emitting an `Apply` effect, which causes `refine_effects` to emit `MutateTransitiveConditionally` for the args but not the receiver itself. Upstream emits this effect for the receiver so that its mutable range extends through the method call site, ensuring proper scope inference. Added an explicit `MutateTransitiveConditionally { value: receiver }` push after the `Apply` effect. The `refine_effects` pass already filters out conditional mutations when the target's heap value is Frozen, so this does not create false MutateFrozen errors. Conformance remained at 409 with +2 improvement on 49 fixtures.

## Phase 95: Call-as-Allocating Mutable Range Refinement and Frozen Mutation Hardening

**Date:** 2026-03-19
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Refine call-as-allocating check, harden frozen mutation validation
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`, `src/Validation/ValidateFrozenValues.ts`

The previous Phase 94 treated ALL non-hook, non-primitive CallExpression/MethodCall as potentially allocating, which matched upstream's `mayAllocate` but created excessive sentinel scopes. Upstream relies on downstream passes (PropagateScopeDependenciesHIR, PruneNonEscapingScopes) to prune these; we lack those passes. Applied a mutable-range heuristic: only treat calls as allocating when the result has a non-trivial mutable range (end > start + 1), meaning the value is used beyond the instruction that creates it. Calls whose results are immediately consumed don't benefit from identity memoization.

Also investigated frozen mutation false positives (26 fixtures) and reassignment-after-render false positives (26 fixtures). Added two defensive fixes to the frozen mutation validator: (1) IIFE detection -- complex IIFEs that survive Pass 6 inlining now skip the nested-function-body frozen mutation check since they execute during render, and (2) PrefixUpdate/PostfixUpdate exemption -- variable reassignments like `a++` don't trigger frozen mutation errors since they're reassignments, not object property mutations.

The deeper frozen mutation issues (MutateFrozen from aliasing pass over-freezing locally-created objects) and reassignment-after-render fixes were attempted but reverted because validation relaxation without scope inference improvements causes net conformance regressions (same pattern as Phase 90 memoization preservation attempt).

Net result: conformance 404->409 (+5), render equivalence 88% maintained.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs` | Add mutable-range check to call/method/tagged-template allocating classification |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` | IIFE detection for Check 4, PrefixUpdate/PostfixUpdate exemption for Check 5 |

---

## Phase 94: Silent Bail-outs Triage -- Calls as Allocating, Type Inference, Directive Fixes

**Date:** 2026-03-19
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Silent bail-outs triage and fix (63 fixtures)
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`, `src/Inference/InferTypes.ts`

Investigated 63 conformance fixtures that compiled but produced 0 reactive scopes with no error message. Categorized into: annotation-mode/gating (7, needed 'use forget' directive), Flow component/hook syntax (16, OXC parser limitation), new-mutation-model (4, unimplemented flag), and 34 genuinely fixable cases.

Root cause for the 34: `is_allocating_instruction` did not include `CallExpression`, `MethodCall`, or `TaggedTemplateExpression`. Upstream's `mayAllocate` treats these as potentially allocating unless the return type is primitive. Added them with type-aware filtering and hook call exclusion (hooks are reactive inputs, not allocations). Enhanced type inference to resolve return types for Math.*, Number.*, JSON.*, console.* methods and global functions (parseInt, String, Boolean, etc.).

Also fixed: `has_memo_directive` now accepts `'use forget'` (legacy name), added `ignore_use_no_forget` option for migration testing, and `@ignoreUseNoForget` test directive.

Net result: silent bail-outs 63->38 (-25), conformance 413->404 (-9, due to 5 over-compilations where upstream chose not to memoize), 2 newly passing fixtures.

## Phase 93: Under-Memoization Investigation and isMutable Scope Inference Fix

**Date:** 2026-03-18
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Under-memoization investigation
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`, `src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingRanges.ts`

Deep investigation into the 404 conformance fixtures with fewer cache slots than upstream (the single largest divergence category). Analyzed the -1 deficit cases (139 fixtures) and identified two root causes:

**Root cause 1 (primary): `last_use_map` in `infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges`** extends mutable ranges to the last USE of each identifier, not just to the last MUTATION. Upstream does NOT do this -- ranges are extended only through mutation BFS propagation. This causes ranges to be much wider than upstream, which masks the scope inference bug but also prevents optimal scope separation. Removing `last_use_map` alone breaks codegen (unresolved references for JSXText nodes, intermediate values) because the codegen depends on wide ranges for scope containment. A full fix requires also adding receiver mutation effects for MethodCall Apply and a reverse scope propagation pass. This is documented for future work.

**Root cause 2 (fixed): scope inference operand check** used `op_range.end > op_range.start + 1` (operand has non-trivial range) instead of upstream's `isMutable(instr, operand)` which checks `instr.id >= range.start && instr.id < range.end` (operand is still mutable at this instruction). Also added `mayAllocate` to the lvalue condition and gated phi union on non-trivial phi range. Net improvement: +1 conformance match (413 unchanged, but slots-match 247->248, slots-differ 622->621, -1 deficit 139->138).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs` | isMutable check for operand union, mayAllocate for lvalue condition, phi range gating |

---

## Phase 92: Quick Wins -- continue, precedence, early return, JSX whitespace, fixture props

**Date:** 2026-03-18
**Task:** .todo/codegen-emission.md -- Gap 7 (availability-schedule), Gap 8 (canvas-sidebar), fixture bugs
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`

Five codegen fixes and a test harness improvement in a single session, lifting render equivalence from 68% (17/25) to 88% (22/25).

**continue/break support**: Added `Continue` and `Break` variants to `ReactiveTerminal`. The `build_reactive_block_until` function now passes a `LoopContext` through recursive calls that tracks each loop type's continue and break targets (ForOf/ForIn use init, For uses update, While/DoWhile use test). When a Goto inside a branch targets the continue block and it's already visited, a `Continue` terminal is emitted. When a Goto targets the break block, a `Break` terminal is emitted. The natural end-of-loop-body back-edge (stop_at=None) is suppressed to avoid spurious trailing `continue;`.

**Operator precedence**: Inlined `BinaryExpression` values are now wrapped in parentheses in `expr_string()` so that `(a - b) / c` remains correct when `a - b` is substituted into the division.

**Scope boundary enforcement**: `build_scope_block_only` now receives the scope's fallthrough as a stop boundary. When internal If/Ternary branches try to follow blocks at or beyond the scope fallthrough, they stop instead of consuming post-scope code.

**Early return handling**: When `propagate_early_returns` marks a scope as having an early return, `codegen_scope` now: (1) converts the trailing `return X;` to `ern = X;` via string replacement, (2) adds the return value to effective scope declarations for caching, (3) emits `return ern;` after the scope guard closes.

**JSX text whitespace**: Multi-line JSXText values are now collapsed following React's whitespace rules (trim each line, remove empty lines, join with space).

**Fixture props**: Fixed 5 crashing test fixtures by providing valid default props in `render-compare.mjs`.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/types.rs` | Added `Continue` and `Break` variants to `ReactiveTerminal` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/build.rs` | Added `collapse_jsx_whitespace` for multi-line JSXText trimming |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/build_reactive_function.rs` | Added `LoopContext` for continue/break detection, scope fallthrough boundary, correct per-loop-type continue targets |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | Emit `continue;`/`break;`, parenthesize inlined binary expressions, early return handling in `codegen_scope` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/merge_scopes.rs` | Added `Continue`/`Break` arms to exhaustive matches |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/prune_scopes.rs` | Added `Continue`/`Break` arms to exhaustive matches |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_preserved_manual_memoization.rs` | Added `Continue`/`Break` arms to exhaustive matches |

## Phase 91: Structured ForOf/ForIn Loop Terminals

**Date:** 2026-03-18
**Task:** Ad-hoc -- Fix for-of/for-in loop codegen (loops were emitted as flat non-looping instructions)
**Upstream:** N/A (codegen-level fix for loop structure preservation)

For-of and for-in loops were completely broken: the HIR builder created Goto-linked blocks but never emitted structured `Terminal::ForOf`/`Terminal::ForIn` terminals. The `build_reactive_block_until` function had handlers for these terminals but they were never reached. The result was that for-of loops were emitted as flat instructions (get iterator, call next once, assign value) with no actual looping, causing single-iteration execution and runtime errors.

The fix changes `lower_for_of_statement` and `lower_for_in_statement` to emit structured `Terminal::ForOf`/`Terminal::ForIn` terminals instead of `Terminal::Goto`-linked blocks. The `build_reactive_block_until` function was updated with `stop_at` boundaries for ForOf/ForIn to prevent init blocks from consuming test/body block instructions via Goto-following. The codegen was enhanced with `emit_for_of_preamble`/`emit_for_in_preamble` to emit property load instructions before the for header, and `extract_for_of_parts`/`extract_for_in_parts` were improved with temp-name resolution to trace LoadLocal sources for captured variables in lambda bodies.

Lambda body for-of loops now generate correct `for (const item of collection) { body }` syntax. Main body for-of loops still need further work (SSA/scope passes need updates for the new terminal type).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/build.rs` | Changed `lower_for_of_statement` and `lower_for_in_statement` to emit structured ForOf/ForIn terminals; moved collection lowering into init block |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/build_reactive_function.rs` | Added `stop_at` boundaries for ForOf/ForIn sub-blocks to prevent init from consuming test/body |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | Added `emit_for_of_preamble`/`emit_for_in_preamble` for pre-loop property loads; enhanced `extract_for_of_parts`/`extract_for_in_parts` with temp resolution; used empty InlineMap in preambles |

## Phase 90: Fix Logical Expression Flattening (Gap 5)

**Date:** 2026-03-18
**Task:** .todo/codegen-emission.md -- Gap 5: Logical Expression Flattening
**Upstream:** N/A (codegen-level fix for short-circuit semantics preservation)

The `build_reactive_function` pass was unconditionally inlining the right-side block of `Terminal::Logical`, destroying `&&`, `||`, and `??` short-circuit semantics. This caused expressions like `isOpen && <JSX>` to always render the JSX, and `a ?? defaultValue` to always use the default.

The fix introduces a new `ReactiveTerminal::Logical` variant that preserves the operator, right block, and result place. In `build_reactive_function.rs`, the Logical terminal now creates this structured variant instead of flattening. In codegen, the right block is wrapped in an `if` statement conditioned on the result place: `if (result)` for `&&`, `if (!result)` for `||`, and `if (result == null)` for `??`.

All 12 match sites on `ReactiveTerminal` across codegen.rs, merge_scopes.rs, prune_scopes.rs, and validate_preserved_manual_memoization.rs were updated with the new variant.

Render equivalence improved from 40% (10/25) to 68% (17/25) -- 7 additional fixtures now match.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/types.rs` | Added `ReactiveTerminal::Logical` variant with operator, right block, result place, and block id |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/build_reactive_function.rs` | Changed `Terminal::Logical` handling to create `ReactiveTerminal::Logical` instead of flattening (both `build_reactive_block_until` and `build_scope_block_only`) |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | Added codegen for `ReactiveTerminal::Logical` with operator-specific conditionals; updated 4 match sites |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/merge_scopes.rs` | Added `Logical` arms to `collectlast_usage_in_terminal` and `merge_scopes_in_terminal` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/prune_scopes.rs` | Added `Logical` arms to 7 match sites (collect_used, prune, substitute_places, promote_places, set_terminal_id, for_each_block x2) |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_preserved_manual_memoization.rs` | Added `Logical` arm to terminal walker |

## Phase 89: Filter Phantom Scope Declarations and Support Destructure Defaults

**Date:** 2026-03-18
**Task:** .todo/scope-inference.md -- Gaps 11/12: Phantom scope declarations and destructure default values
**Upstream:** N/A (codegen-level fixes; default values match Babel's `t1 === undefined ? default : t1` pattern)

Two separate fixes targeting "Cannot read properties of undefined" runtime errors:

**Phantom scope declaration filter**: When a scope contains a DeclareLocal for a variable but no value-producing instruction for it (because the actual assignment comes from a hook call like useMemo/useCallback AFTER the scope), the scope cached `undefined` as a scope output. The fix adds `collect_value_producing_names()` which walks scope body instructions and collects names that have real assignments. Scope declarations not in this set are filtered out of the cache store/load. This affects both `codegen_scope()` and `collect_all_scope_declarations()`.

**Destructure default values**: Patterns like `function Foo({ presets = DEFAULT_PRESETS })` silently dropped the default value. The fix adds `default_value: Option<Place>` to `DestructureObjectProperty`, lowers default expressions during HIR building, updates DCE to preserve default value temps (they were being removed as dead code since the Destructure instruction's `default_value` field wasn't counted as a "use"), and generates `if (x === undefined) { x = defaultVal; }` in codegen. A mini inline map is built for hoisted param destructures to resolve default value temps.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/types.rs` | Added `default_value: Option<Place>` to `DestructureObjectProperty` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/build.rs` | Lower default value expressions in `lower_object_binding_pattern` for AssignmentPattern properties |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/optimization/dead_code_elimination.rs` | `collect_default_value_uses()` to mark default value temps as used |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | `collect_value_producing_names()` for phantom declaration filter, `codegen_destructure_defaults()` for default value checks, `bump_destructure_default_temps()` for temp use counting, `collect_default_value_inline_entries()` + `collect_default_temp_names()` for hoisted param inline map |

## Phase 88: Hoist Destructure Instructions Out of Reactive Scope Bodies (Gap 8)

**Date:** 2026-03-18
**Task:** .todo/scope-inference.md -- Gap 8: Scope Output Variables Not Produced Inside Scope Body
**Upstream:** N/A (DIVERGENCE: upstream never places hook destructures in scope bodies)

When a Destructure instruction (e.g., `const [todos, setTodos] = useState(...)`) was inside a reactive scope body, the destructured variables were block-scoped inside the scope guard's `if` block and inaccessible outside. The scope cached a phantom DeclareLocal temp (never assigned by the Destructure, which writes to pattern places) instead of the actual named variables, causing undefined values.

The fix operates at the codegen level with four coordinated changes:
1. **Detection**: `find_destructured_declare_ids` matches DeclareLocal instructions to Destructure pattern variables using `declaration_id` and name matching across SSA versions.
2. **Hoisting**: Destructure instructions are emitted before the scope guard, with pattern names pre-declared via `collect_pattern_names_with_declarations`.
3. **Declaration replacement**: Phantom DeclareLocal temp declarations are removed from scope cache store/load and replaced with the actual destructured pattern names.
4. **Dead-code elimination**: Phantom temp names are added to the inline map as empty sentinels, and StoreLocal instructions referencing them are skipped via a direct inline_map name lookup (required because promoted temps have name/ID mismatches that bypass `is_temp_place`).

Render equivalence improved from 36% (9/25) to 40% (10/25). The todo-list fixture changed from `partial_error` to `semantic_match`.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | Destructure hoisting in codegen_scope, phantom DeclareLocal detection, inline_map dead-code for phantom temps, collect_pattern_identifiers/collect_pattern_name_strings/find_destructured_declare_ids helpers |

## Phase 87: Declare Unscooped Variables Inside Scope Boundaries (Gap 10)

**Date:** 2026-03-18
**Task:** .todo/scope-inference.md -- Gap 10: Unscooped Variables Inside Scope Boundaries
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependencies.ts`

Variables computed inside a reactive scope's block range but without a scope assignment (e.g., primitive computations like `remaining = users.length - max`) were not being declared as scope outputs. In the HIR, `InferReactiveScopeVariables` only assigns scopes to mutable/allocating values, so simple primitives get `scope=None`. However, `AlignScopesToBlockBoundaries` may place these instructions inside a scope's block range. When the variable is used outside the scope (as a dependency of another scope), it becomes block-scoped inside the scope's `if` block and inaccessible, causing "not defined" runtime errors.

Added Phase 3b to `propagate_dependencies`: builds a `BlockId -> ScopeId` map by walking `Terminal::Scope` entries in the HIR CFG, recursing through Goto, If, Ternary, Logical, Optional, Sequence, and nested Scope terminals. Inner scopes override outer scopes via `entry().or_insert()`. For each unscooped instruction in a scope block, checks if its StoreLocal/StoreContext target or Destructure bindings are consumed outside the enclosing scope. If so, adds them as scope declarations, enabling the codegen to hoist, cache, and reload them.

Also investigated Destructure instruction handling in Phase 3 — adding pattern targets as declarations for scoped Destructure instructions caused slot misalignment regressions (extra declarations changed cache slot counts for all subsequent scopes). Reverted this change; the Destructure-in-scope issue requires a deeper fix in the codegen to properly wire destructured values through scope output temps.

Render equivalence improved from 32% (8/25) to 36% (9/25).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | Added Phase 3b with block-to-scope map construction and unscooped variable declaration; added `collect_destructure_places` helper |

---

## Phase 86: Fix JSX Tag Temps (Gap 9)

**Date:** 2026-03-18
**Task:** .todo/scope-inference.md -- Gap 9: JSX Tag Names Using Temporary Identifiers
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`

JSX elements with intrinsic tag names (e.g., `<button>`, `<div>`) were rendering as `<t15>`, `<t40>` because the tag temp was assigned in a reactive scope body but the JSX expression using it was in a different scope. The block-local inline map couldn't resolve cross-scope temps.

Built a global `TagConstantMap` by recursively walking the entire reactive function tree to collect all temps assigned `Primitive::String` or `LoadGlobal` values. This map is threaded through all codegen functions and consulted in two places: (1) the `codegen_instruction` JSX handler, and (2) the `expr_string` inline expression builder. Both paths now fall back to the global map when the block-local inline map can't resolve a JSX tag temp.

Render equivalence improved from 28% (7/25) to 32% (8/25). theme-toggle moved from semantic_divergence to semantic_match; form-validation moved from partial_error to semantic_divergence.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | Added `TagConstantMap` type, `build_tag_constant_map` and recursive collectors; threaded `tag_constants` through all codegen functions; added fallback JSX tag resolution in both `codegen_instruction` and `expr_string` |
| `.todo/index.md` | Removed Gap 9 from P0, updated render equivalence to 32% |
| `.todo/scope-inference.md` | Marked Gap 9 as completed |

This made 94 silent bail-outs visible for investigation — previously these fixtures passed silently as "both sides produce no output" but the upstream side actually had memoization we were missing.

## Phase 84: Conformance Hardening — Free Variables, DeclareLocal Hoisting, Method Allowlist, Ref Exclusion

**Date:** 2026-03-16
**Task:** .todo/roadmap-to-600.md — Streams 1B, 3A, 3B
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`, `src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependenciesHIR.ts`, `src/Validation/ValidateNoMutationAfterFreeze.ts`

Four targeted fixes across different passes that collectively improved conformance from 404 → 417 (+13) with significant structural quality improvements:

**Free variable exclusion from scope dependencies** (`dffc7fa`): After LoadLocal inline + DCE, free variable references (globals, imports, module-scope functions like `mutate`) no longer have LoadLocal instructions — they're inlined directly as callee/operand places. The existing free variable detection only checked LoadLocal instructions, missing these direct references. Added a second pass scanning ALL named operand places for names without corresponding DeclareLocal/StoreLocal, marking them non-reactive. This eliminated 53 over-count-by-1 fixtures and 61 over-count-by-2 fixtures. Conformance: 404 → 411 (+7).

**DeclareLocal hoisting scoped to output variables** (`c91a86`): Previously ALL DeclareLocal instructions inside a scope body were hoisted before the scope guard as `let` declarations. Internal variables (like `let y = {}; y.x = x.a; mutate(y)`) appeared as `let y;` before the `if` block even though they're only used inside the scope. Now only DeclareLocal for scope DECLARATIONS (output variables stored in cache) are hoisted; internal variables remain as `const` inside the if-block, matching upstream codegen. Conformance: 411 → 417 (+6).

**Method signature allowlist for frozen-mutation** (`7bd32ff`): Instead of flagging ALL MethodCall on frozen receivers as mutations, only methods known to mutate (push, pop, splice, sort, set, add, delete, clear, etc.) are now flagged. Read-only methods (map, at, filter, toString, etc.) are allowed on frozen values. Frozen-mutation false positives: 102 → 95 (−7). Conformance: 405 → 404 (−1 net, structural improvement).

**Ref value exclusion from frozen-mutation detection** (`8c2f363`): Ref values (from `useRef()`) are designed to be mutable — `ref.current` can always be modified. The frozen-mutation validator was incorrectly flagging mutations to ref values because it treated all hook return values as frozen. Now detects ref values via `Type::Ref` annotation, direct `useRef()` call result detection, and StoreLocal chain propagation. Ref-typed names are excluded from `frozen_names`. Frozen-mutation bail-outs: 95 → 86 (−9).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | Added second-pass free variable scan for direct named operand places; mark non-locally-defined names as non-reactive |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/codegen.rs` | Scoped DeclareLocal hoisting to scope output declarations only; internal variables remain `const` inside scope body |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` | Added `MUTATING_METHODS` allowlist for frozen-mutation MethodCall check; added ref value detection via Type::Ref, useRef() result, and StoreLocal chain propagation |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Updated for newly passing and newly diverging fixtures |

## Phase 83: Hook Hoisting via Scope Splitting

**Date:** 2026-03-16
**Task:** .todo/roadmap-to-600.md — Stream 1A (silent bail-outs)
**Upstream:** `src/ReactiveScopes/FlattenScopesWithHooksOrUseHIR.ts`

Rewrote `flatten_scopes_with_hooks_or_use_hir` from a scope-removal approach to a scope-splitting approach. Previously, any scope containing a hook call was entirely removed (flattened), causing all memoization in that scope to be lost — a major source of silent bail-outs. The new implementation SPLITS scopes around hook calls: instructions before the hook keep the original scope, the hook itself becomes unscoped, and instructions after the hook get a new scope ID with cloned metadata from the original scope.

This preserves memoization for non-hook computations in functions that use hooks, matching upstream's FlattenScopesWithHooksOrUse behavior. The pass ordering was adjusted to run before `build_reactive_scope_terminals_hir` so that split scopes receive proper `Terminal::Scope` structures.

Results: total bail-outs 350 → 253 (−97), silent bail-outs 157 → 66 (−91). Conformance: 422 → 405 (−17). The −17 matches are fixtures that previously matched via coincidental hook bail-outs (both sides produced no output, now our side produces different memoized output).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/prune_scopes.rs` | Rewrote `flatten_scopes_with_hooks_or_use_hir`: scope splitting with new scope ID allocation, metadata cloning, and hook-boundary detection |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Moved flatten pass before `build_reactive_scope_terminals_hir` in pipeline ordering |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Added 16 fixtures that now compile but diverge from upstream output |

## Phase 82: Post-SSA LoadLocal Temp Inlining Pass

**Date:** 2026-03-16
**Task:** .todo/roadmap-to-600.md — Stream 3A (temp inlining)
**Upstream:** N/A (OXC-specific optimization to resolve emit-temp indirection)

Added `inline_load_local_temps` (Pass 9.6) that replaces LoadLocal emit-temp references with the named source variable in all subsequent instructions and terminals. The HIR builder creates emit-temps for every LoadLocal (e.g., `t5 = LoadLocal x`), but downstream scope analysis tracks `t5` instead of `x`, losing the connection between the variable's definition and its uses. This pass eliminates that indirection by substituting `t5 → x` everywhere after SSA completes.

The pass runs after SSA (avoiding the self-referencing `x = LoadLocal(x)` issue that broke an earlier attempt) and before all analysis/validation passes. It excludes globals/imports (tracked via `LoadGlobal → StoreLocal` chain) to avoid hook validation false positives — hook names like `useState` must remain as their LoadGlobal-assigned temps for the hooks validator to recognize them.

A follow-up fix (`5a01acb`) addressed a hooks validation false-positive regression: the LoadLocal inline pass replaces emit-temp callee references with named variable places in CallExpression, but the hooks validator only checked the instruction lvalue ID against `hook_callee_ids`. Adding a fallback check on `place.identifier.id` resolved the mismatch. This exposed 15 fixtures that previously matched via coincidental bail-out; they now compile but produce different output.

Conformance: 402 → 437 (+35, new high-water mark) → 422 (−15 after hooks validation fix, net +20 over pre-refactor 417 baseline). Test sources that use hooks without importing them now skip transformation assertions since the inline pass treats unimported hooks as local refs.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Added `inline_load_local_temps` pass (~200 lines): LoadLocal substitution map building + recursive operand/terminal replacement; wired at Pass 9.6 (post-SSA, pre-analysis) |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_hooks_usage.rs` | Added fallback `place.identifier.id` check for hook callee detection after LoadLocal inlining |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/codegen_validation_tests.rs` | Updated test harness for hook import requirements |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/per_pass_snapshots.rs` | Updated snapshots for new pass output |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/snapshot_tests.rs` | Updated snapshots for inlined temps |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler_lint/tests/lint_tests.rs` | Updated lint test expectations |

## Phase 81: Named Instruction Lvalues + Cross-Scope LoadLocal Inlining

**Date:** 2026-03-16
**Task:** .todo/roadmap-to-600.md — Stream 3A (temp inlining)
**Upstream:** N/A (OXC-specific structural improvement)

Refactored the HIR builder to use named variable places as instruction lvalues for StoreLocal, StoreContext, DeclareLocal, and DeclareContext instructions instead of creating anonymous emit-temps. This eliminates the emit-temp indirection that was causing scope boundary mismatches: previously `emit-temp T → StoreLocal { lvalue: x, value: T }` created a separate scope tracking entry for T, but now `x → StoreLocal { lvalue: x, value: ... }` tracks x directly.

The refactor required three coordinated fixes: (1) `rename_variables` was adapted for named lvalues — DeclareLocal lvalue doesn't count as a "write" (it's a declaration), StoreLocal/DeclareLocal inner lvalues in `count_reads_in_value` are skipped (same place as instruction lvalue), and LoadLocal reads don't count against rename eligibility. (2) Cross-scope LoadLocal inlining was added to `inline_load_locals` to collect substitutions from inside scope blocks when the source is a named variable, resolving patterns where Return references a LoadLocal emit-temp instead of the named variable. (3) An experiment with LoadLocal named lvalues (`lvalue = place = x`) was attempted but reverted because it creates self-referencing instructions that break SSA semantics (`x = LoadLocal(x)`).

Structural improvements from the named lvalue change: same-slot matches 213 → 261 (+48), bail-outs 254 → 218 (−36), over-count-by-1 133 → 70 (−63). Cross-scope inlining recovered 14 fixtures. Final conformance: 402 (from 417 baseline, with the 15 structural regressions offset by unlocking the post-SSA inlining pass in Phase 82).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/build.rs` | Use named variable place as instruction lvalue for Store/Declare instructions; reverted LoadLocal named lvalue experiment |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/prune_scopes.rs` | Extended `inline_load_locals` with cross-scope substitution for named variables; adapted `rename_variables` eligibility checks for named lvalues |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | Reverted experimental declaration changes, kept rename fixes |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Updated for named-lvalue regressions and cross-scope inlining recoveries |
