## Phase 80: Param-ID Reactive Seeding with Mutable Value Gate

**Date:** 2026-03-16
**Task:** .todo/stable-identifier-ids.md — Reactivity seeding with stable IDs
**Upstream:** `src/Inference/InferReactivePlaces.ts`, `src/ReactiveScopes/InferReactiveScopeVariables.ts`

Two coordinated changes that reduce silent bail-outs by enabling correct param-derived reactivity tracking with stable IdentifierIds:

**Pipeline plumbing** (`43a6243`): Extracted `IdentifierId`s from `HIRFunction.params` and threaded them through `run_pipeline` to `infer_reactive_places`. This prepares the infrastructure for direct param seeding rather than relying on DeclareLocal instructions in the entry block (which was fragile with stable IDs since not all params necessarily have entry-block DeclareLocal).

**Param seeding activation** (`19ffc69`): Two changes that work together — (1) `infer_reactive_places` now seeds param IdentifierIds as reactive directly (not just via DeclareLocal in entry block), and (2) `infer_reactive_scope_variables` adds an `is_mutable_instruction` check that includes CallExpression/MethodCall alongside allocating instructions. Scope creation now requires `any_allocating || (any_reactive && any_mutable)` instead of `any_reactive || any_allocating`. This prevents over-memoization of primitives-only functions (e.g., `function foo(x) { return x; }`) where param reactivity alone shouldn't trigger scope creation.

Results: silent bail-outs 94 → 70 (−24), total bail-outs 279 → 254 (−25), same-slot matches 178 → 213 (+35). Conformance: 418 → 417 (−1, net neutral — the structural alignment improvements are significant despite the neutral match count).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Extract param IdentifierIds and thread through pipeline to infer_reactive_places |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_reactive_places.rs` | Seed param IDs directly as reactive in fixpoint loop |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/infer_reactive_scope_variables.rs` | Added `is_mutable_instruction` check; scope creation requires `any_allocating \|\| (any_reactive && any_mutable)` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/pass_unit_tests.rs` | Updated unit test expectations for new seeding behavior |

## Phase 79: Scope-Aware Stable IdentifierIds (Revert + Re-implement)

**Date:** 2026-03-16
**Task:** .todo/stable-identifier-ids.md — Scope-aware retry
**Upstream:** N/A (OXC-specific architectural fix)

The Phase 78 stable IdentifierId refactor used a flat `binding_ids: FxHashMap<String, ...>` registry that conflated shadowed bindings — a variable `x` in an inner block would share the same IdentifierId as an outer `x`, breaking scope analysis and preserve-memo validation. This phase went through a revert-and-re-implement cycle to fix the root cause.

**Revert** (`f161523`): Removed the `binding_ids` registry and `ssa_version` field. Kept the SSA pass improvements (cleaner phi elimination, version tracking). **Re-apply + scope-aware fix** (`c818296` + `7915874`): Replaced the flat registry with a scope stack (`binding_scopes: Vec<FxHashMap<...>>`) that correctly handles JavaScript lexical scoping. `push_scope()`/`pop_scope()` are called at block statements, for-loops, and for-in/of loops. `make_declared_place()` for declarations (let/const/var/param) always creates a fresh binding in the current scope frame. `make_named_place()` for references looks up innermost-to-outermost. Shadowed variables correctly get distinct IdentifierIds while all references to the same binding share one ID.

Conformance: 424 → 418 (−6). The delta comes from preserve-memo-validation fixtures where stable IDs change scope analysis behavior. 8 regressions documented as known limitations (temp renaming + preserve-memo patterns).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/build.rs` | Replaced flat `binding_ids` with `binding_scopes: Vec<FxHashMap<...>>` scope stack; added `push_scope()`/`pop_scope()`; `make_declared_place()` creates fresh binding in current frame; `make_named_place()` looks up innermost-to-outermost |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/types.rs` | `ssa_version: u32` field on `Identifier` (retained from Phase 78) |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/ssa/enter_ssa.rs` | SSA rewrite retained from Phase 78: version stacks, `fresh_ssa_version()`, helper fn removal |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/ssa/eliminate_redundant_phi.rs` | `SsaId = (IdentifierId, u32)` tuple-based replacement (retained from Phase 78) |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/compute_unconditional_blocks.rs` | `ssa_version: 0` at Identifier construction sites |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/collect_hoistable_property_loads.rs` | `ssa_version: 0` at Identifier construction site |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/collect_optional_chain_dependencies.rs` | `ssa_version: 0` at Identifier construction site |

| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/scope_dependency_utils.rs` | `ssa_version: 0` at Identifier construction site |

## Phase 78: Stable IdentifierId Refactor

**Date:** 2026-03-16
**Task:** .todo/stable-identifier-ids.md -- All phases (1–7)
**Upstream:** N/A (OXC-specific architectural fix)

The HIR was assigning a fresh `IdentifierId` to every `Place` created for a variable reference. A variable `x` referenced five times would have five distinct IDs, making it structurally impossible for downstream passes (freeze tracking, mutation, alias analysis) to correlate state across references to the same binding. This phase implements a stable-ID architecture across three coordinated sub-phases.

**Phase 1 (Types & Builder):** Added `ssa_version: u32` to the `Identifier` struct to carry the SSA rename index separately from the base identity. Added a `binding_ids: FxHashMap<String, (IdentifierId, DeclarationId)>` registry to `HIRBuilder`; `make_named_place()` now looks up or inserts into this registry so all references to the same binding share one `IdentifierId`. Temporaries via `make_temp()` still get fresh IDs. Updated all 15 `Identifier` construction sites across 9 files to include `ssa_version: 0`. The `InstructionValue` size assertion was bumped from 256 to 264 bytes to reflect the added field. **Phase 2 (SSA Rewrite):** Rewrote `enter_ssa.rs` to operate on `(IdentifierId, version)` pairs: version stacks are `FxHashMap<IdentifierId, Vec<u32>>`, `fresh_ssa_name()` became `fresh_ssa_version()` returning a `u32`, and phi operand matching uses the base `IdentifierId` directly. Removed three helper functions (`find_max_identifier_id`, `find_declaration_id_for_var`, `find_name_for_var`) that existed solely to work around the fresh-ID scheme. Rewrote `eliminate_redundant_phi.rs` to use `SsaId = (IdentifierId, u32)` tuples in its replacement map instead of `IdentifierId → IdentifierId`. **Phase 3–7 (Verification):** Audited all downstream passes (inference, reactive scopes, validation, optimization, codegen). No changes were needed: maps keyed by `IdentifierId` now have one entry per variable (correct semantics), temporaries retain unique IDs (no naming collision in codegen), and mutable ranges become slightly more conservative (wider) but semantically correct. All 160 unit tests pass; conformance holds at 1293 known failures (no regressions — this is a foundational correctness change, not a conformance fix).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/types.rs` | Added `ssa_version: u32` field to `Identifier`; bumped `InstructionValue` size assertion 256 → 264 |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/build.rs` | Added `binding_ids` registry; `make_named_place()` reuses stable `IdentifierId`/`DeclarationId` per binding name |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/ssa/enter_ssa.rs` | Complete rewrite: version stacks use `u32`; `fresh_ssa_version()` replaces `fresh_ssa_name()`; three helper fns removed |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/ssa/eliminate_redundant_phi.rs` | `SsaId = (IdentifierId, u32)` tuple-based replacement map replacing `IdentifierId → IdentifierId` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/compute_unconditional_blocks.rs` | Added `ssa_version: 0` to `Identifier` construction sites |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/collect_hoistable_property_loads.rs` | Added `ssa_version: 0` to `Identifier` construction site |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/collect_optional_chain_dependencies.rs` | Added `ssa_version: 0` to `Identifier` construction site |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/optimization/optimize_props_method_calls.rs` | Added `ssa_version: 0` to `Identifier` construction site |

| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/scope_dependency_utils.rs` | Added `ssa_version: 0` to `Identifier` construction site |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | Added `ssa_version: 0` to `Identifier` construction site |

## Phase 77: Hybrid Effects+Instruction Frozen-Mutation Validator Rewrite

**Date:** 2026-03-16
**Task:** .todo/false-bailouts.md -- Frozen-mutation false positives
**Upstream:** `src/Validation/ValidateNoMutationAfterFreeze.ts`

Rewrote `validate_no_mutation_after_freeze` from a 925-line name-based frozen tracking implementation to a ~335-line hybrid approach. The new design has two complementary layers: (1) effects-based detection using `MutateFrozen` effects emitted by the abstract interpreter during `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects`, and (2) targeted instruction-level checks for edge cases that the effects layer cannot express. The effects layer handles the common case of direct mutations on frozen values. The instruction-level layer covers three specific patterns: `MethodCall` receiver mutations (which cannot be expressed as effects without changing scope analysis for all method calls), `PropertyStore` on frozen targets, and nested function bodies that close over frozen values.

Hook return value pre-freezing and hook call capture freezing were also refined. The root cause of the previous over-flagging was the fresh-ID-per-reference architecture: because each reference to a variable gets a fresh abstract heap ID, the heap cannot link freeze state across references without a pre-linking step. The earlier attempt to pre-link by name forced all IDs to `Mutable` in the lattice, causing cascading false positives in other passes. The hybrid approach sidesteps this by using effects (which are already resolved to the correct IDs by the abstract interpreter) for the common case and falling back to instruction-level name matching only for the three patterns that genuinely require it. Additionally, the `Apply` fallback in `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects` emits `MutateTransitiveConditionally` for all arguments including frozen params; the validator now skips conditional mutations for `CallExpression`/`MethodCall` instructions to avoid those false positives. Net result: frozen-mutation false-positive bail-outs dropped 158 → 89 (−69), total bail-outs 312 → 258 (−54). Conformance moved 435 → 424 (−11): 4 real regressions requiring alias/phi/derivation-chain tracking to fix, and 7 pre-existing divergences that were previously masked by the false bail-outs and are now visible.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` | Full rewrite: ~925 lines → ~335 lines; effects-based detection + targeted instruction-level checks for MethodCall/PropertyStore/nested functions |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` | Minor cleanup |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | +11 entries for newly visible pre-existing divergences and real regressions |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__basic_memoization.snap` | Updated for validator output changes |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__conditional_rendering.snap` | Updated for validator output changes |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__hook_dependencies.snap` | Updated for validator output changes |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__multiple_scopes.snap` | Updated for validator output changes |
| `tests/snapshots/snapshot_tests__hook_with_use_state.snap` | Updated for validator output changes |

## Phase 76: Gate setState Name Heuristic Behind `enableTreatSetIdentifiersAsStateSetters`

**Date:** 2026-03-15
**Task:** .todo/false-bailouts.md -- setState False Positives
**Upstream:** `src/Validation/ValidateNoSetStateInRender.ts`

Fixed 11 false-positive setState-during-render bail-outs caused by the `is_set_state_name()` heuristic matching imported utility functions like `setProperty` and `setPropertyByKey` from `shared-runtime`. The heuristic (which matches any `setXxx` name where X is uppercase) was always enabled, but upstream only enables it with the `enableTreatSetIdentifiersAsStateSetters` config flag, which defaults to false.

The fix had three parts: (1) Changed the `enable_treat_set_identifiers_as_state_setters` default from `true` to `false` in `EnvironmentConfig`, matching upstream. (2) Added a pre-pass in the validator that detects `useState`/`useReducer`/`useTransition`/`useOptimistic`/`useActionState` destructure patterns directly, seeding the `set_state_ids`/`set_state_names` sets from the destructure pattern Places. This was necessary because `infer_types` sets `Type::SetState` on destructure pattern Place IDs that don't match any instruction lvalue ID after SSA renaming, making the type-based detection unreliable. (3) Gated all `is_set_state_name()` calls behind the `enable_name_heuristic` parameter, while keeping the confirmed setState names (from destructure analysis) always active for cross-scope propagation into nested functions. Also added parsing of `@enableTreatSetIdentifiersAsStateSetters` directive in the conformance test harness.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/environment.rs` | Changed `enable_treat_set_identifiers_as_state_setters` default from `true` to `false` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_set_state_in_render.rs` | Added useState destructure pre-pass, gated name heuristic behind config flag, name-based propagation for confirmed setState names |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Thread `enable_treat_set_identifiers_as_state_setters` config to validator |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_types.rs` | Added NOTE about SSA ID mismatch for destructure pattern Places |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/conformance_tests.rs` | Added `@enableTreatSetIdentifiersAsStateSetters` directive parsing |

## Phase 75: `validate_no_unsupported_nodes` Pass + HIR Unsupported Pattern Detection

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/false-bailouts.md -- Unsupported pattern detection gaps
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/HIR/BuildHIR.ts`

Implemented the `validate_no_unsupported_nodes` validation pass, which walks all HIR instructions looking for `UnsupportedNode` values and emits a `CompilerError::todo()` for each one, causing the pipeline to bail out. This matches upstream `BuildHIR.ts` behavior where unsupported syntax patterns are rejected with a `TodoDiagnostic` at lowering time rather than silently compiled. The pass is wired at pipeline Phase 0 (pre-SSA, before any analysis runs) so that the error surfaces immediately without partial analysis artifacts.

Three new unsupported-pattern detection sites were added to `hir/build.rs`. Object getter and setter syntax (`get foo()` / `set foo(v)`) in `ObjectExpression` now lowers to `UnsupportedNode` rather than being silently dropped — these are non-trivial to memoize correctly. `new.target` `MetaProperty` now lowers to `UnsupportedNode` since it is only meaningful inside constructors, which React components cannot be. `for await...of` loops now lower to `UnsupportedNode` because async iteration requires generator protocol semantics the compiler does not model. All three patterns already had upstream `BuildHIR.ts` counterparts that throw `TodoException`.

In `validate_no_global_reassignment.rs`, the JSX prop safety heuristic was narrowed: previously all JSX prop values were treated as safe callback contexts, but the correct upstream behavior is to only suppress the reassignment warning for event-handler props matching the `onXxx` pattern. An unnecessary `FxHashSet::clone()` in the recursive `check_inner_scopes` call was eliminated by passing the existing set by reference. The `MetaProperty` format-string allocation in `build.rs` was also cleaned up — the string was being allocated and immediately dropped without the result being used.

Four previously-failing conformance fixtures began passing: `new-target.js`, `for-await.js`, and two getter/setter object property fixtures. Two pre-existing failures that were incorrectly omitted from `known-failures.txt` were added back. Net conformance: 430 → 434/1717 (+4 fixtures, 0 panics, 0 unexpected divergences).

### New files:

| File | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_unsupported_nodes.rs` | Validation pass that scans all HIR instructions for `UnsupportedNode` values and emits `CompilerError::todo()` bail-out errors |

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/mod.rs` | Added `validate_no_unsupported_nodes` module declaration and re-export |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Wired `validate_no_unsupported_nodes` at Phase 0 (pre-SSA) |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/build.rs` | Added `UnsupportedNode` lowering for object getter/setter syntax, `new.target` MetaProperty, and `for await...of` loops; fixed dead MetaProperty format-string allocation |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_global_reassignment.rs` | Narrowed JSX prop safety check to event-handler props (`onXxx` pattern only); eliminated unnecessary `FxHashSet::clone()` in recursive call |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 4 newly-passing fixtures; added 2 pre-existing failures that were missing |

## Phase 74: `infer_reactive_places` Parameter-Only Seeding Fix

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** Ad-hoc
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferReactivePlaces.ts`

Fixed `infer_reactive_places` to seed reactivity only from function parameters, matching upstream behavior. Previously the entry-block loop would mark every `DeclareLocal` instruction as reactive, including temporaries and locals that had nothing to do with the component's reactive surface. Upstream `InferReactivePlaces.ts` seeds reactivity from `fn.params` — the explicit parameter list — not from arbitrary entry-block declarations.

The fix changed the function signature to accept `param_names: &[String]` and added a guard in the entry-block `DeclareLocal` loop: an instruction is only seeded as reactive if its declared name appears in `param_names`. The call site in `pipeline.rs` already had `param_names` available and was updated to pass it through. Two existing unit test call sites were updated to supply an empty-or-realistic param list. A new unit test `test_infer_reactive_places_only_seeds_params` was added to verify that non-parameter locals in the entry block are not seeded. Five snapshot files were updated to reflect changed cache slot allocation caused by the narrower reactive seed set. Thirty-one fixtures were removed from `known-failures.txt`, moving conformance from 399/1717 (23.2%) to 430/1717 (25.0%), a gain of +31 fixtures.

## Phase 73: `rename_variables` Pass — Scope Output Variable Renaming

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/codegen-structure.md -- scope output variable renaming
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/CodegenReactiveFunction.ts`

Implemented the `rename_variables` pass in `prune_scopes.rs`, which was previously a TODO stub. The pass assigns sequential temp names (`t0`, `t1`, …) to reactive scope declaration outputs, matching the upstream `CodegenReactiveFunction.ts` behavior. For each scope whose output declarations are eligible for renaming, the pass renames the binding to the next temp index and emits a `const originalName = tN` assignment immediately after the scope block so downstream code continues to reference the original name.

The implementation is organized into several helpers. `scan_max_temp_counter` / `scan_max_in_block` walk all existing instructions to find the highest `tN` suffix already in use, preventing collisions with temps generated in earlier passes. `temp_name_index` / `update_max_temp` parse and track those indices. `can_rename_scope_decl` is the main eligibility predicate: a declaration is skipped if it already has a temp name, is a reassignment target, or is read within the scope body (which would require the alias assignment to precede the read — upstream defers this to a later lowering step). `check_rename_eligibility` walks the scope body counting lvalue writes, reads, and detecting reassignment kinds using `InstructionKind`. `count_reads_in_value` and `count_reads_in_terminal` provide exhaustive `InstructionValue` and terminal-operand visitors that count name references, including `Switch` case tests. The pass required adding `InstructionKind` and `Param` to the import block. Two newly passing conformance fixtures were removed from `known-failures.txt`: `array-pattern-params.js` and `object-pattern-params.js`. Conformance moved from 397 → 399/1717 (+2, 0 regressions).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/prune_scopes.rs` | Full implementation of `rename_variables` pass (~380 lines): `scan_max_temp_counter`, `scan_max_in_block`, `temp_name_index`, `update_max_temp`, `can_rename_scope_decl`, `check_rename_eligibility`, `count_reads_in_value`, `count_reads_in_terminal`; added `InstructionKind` and `Param` imports |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 2 newly-passing fixtures: `array-pattern-params.js`, `object-pattern-params.js` |

---

## Phase 72: Arrow Function Preservation in Codegen + Pre-Freeze Infrastructure

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/over-memoization-bailout.md -- Gap 5: Effect Refinement
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/CodegenReactFunction.ts`

Added an `is_arrow: bool` field to both `HIRFunction` and `ReactiveFunction` to preserve whether the original source function was an arrow function. The field is set to `true` in `build_arrow` and `build_arrow_function` in `build.rs`, and threaded through `build_reactive_function`. In `codegen.rs`, `codegen_function` and `codegen_function_with_source_map` branch on `is_arrow` to emit `() => {}` syntax rather than `function() {}`. This unblocked four fixtures where the compiler was emitting regular function syntax for arrow-function components and memo/forwardRef wrappers: `arrow-function-with-implicit-return.js`, `infer-function-React-memo.js`, `infer-function-assignment.js`, and `infer-function-forwardRef.js`. Score moved from 385 → 389/1717 (+4 fixtures).

Separately, pre-freeze infrastructure was added to `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs`: a new `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects_with_params` entry point and a `pre_freeze_params` function that walks all instructions to freeze param-named values in the abstract heap before the main analysis begins. This mirrors the upstream initialization step where component props and hook arguments are frozen at entry. Handlers for `PropertyStore` and `TaggedTemplateExpression` were also fixed per code review. The pipeline in `pipeline.rs` already wires `param_names` to the aliasing pass. A `dump_output.rs` example was added as a quick fixture debug utility for the development workflow.

## Phase 71: Interleaved Fixpoint Loop for InferMutationAliasingEffects

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/over-memoization-bailout.md -- Gap 5: Effect Refinement
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts` (worklist loop pattern)

Refactored `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects` from a sequential 4-phase architecture (collect raw effects → refine → apply to heap → store) into an interleaved fixpoint loop matching the upstream worklist pattern. Each iteration now performs all four steps per-instruction in sequence: compute raw effects, refine using the current heap state, apply to the heap, then store the refined effects on the instruction. The loop repeats over all instructions until no heap state changes are observed, at which point the result has converged.

To enable change tracking, all `AbstractHeap` mutating methods (`create`, `alias`, `capture`, `mutate`, `freeze`) were changed to return `bool` — `true` if the method modified heap state, `false` if the heap was already in the target state. A `merge_value_kinds()` lattice join function was added to support idempotent re-creation: when a place is created a second time with a different `ValueKind`, the function computes the join of the two kinds (`Frozen` ∨ anything = `Frozen`, `Primitive` ∨ `Primitive` = `Primitive`, otherwise `MutableObject`) and returns whether the existing entry was promoted. The dead `Apply` arm in `process_effect_for_heap` was removed — `Apply` effects are fully handled by `refine_effects()` before `process_effect_for_heap` is called, so the arm was unreachable. Documentation comments were added to both the convergence loop and `merge_value_kinds()` explaining the lattice semantics and termination proof (finite place set, monotone join, bounded height). Conformance held at 385/1717 with zero regressions — existing fixtures already converge in a single pass, so the fixpoint loop exits immediately after the first iteration for all current test cases.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` | Refactored to interleaved fixpoint loop; all `AbstractHeap` methods return `bool` for change tracking; added `merge_value_kinds()` lattice join; removed dead `Apply` arm from `process_effect_for_heap`; added convergence + lattice documentation |

---

## Phase 70: Function Signature Resolution for Apply Effects (Iteration 24)

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/over-memoization-bailout.md -- Gap 5: Effect Refinement
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts` (`applyEffect()`), `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/AnalyseFunctions.ts`

`analyse_functions.rs` was completely rewritten to produce a `FxHashMap<IdentifierId, FunctionSignature>` (one entry per function place) rather than the previous flat effect list. The new implementation walks each function's HIR blocks and extracts per-parameter effects: for each parameter it collects all effects that reference that parameter's place, resolving aliases through `StoreLocal`/`LoadLocal`/`TypeCast` chains before attribution. A fixpoint loop propagates signatures transitively — when an inner function calls an outer one whose signature is already known, the callee's parameter effects are inlined into the caller's signature — continuing until no new entries are added. This matches the `AnalyseFunctions.ts` upstream algorithm that builds a stable fixpoint map before any `applyEffect` resolution begins.

The `refine_effects()` phase (Phase 3.5) in `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` implements the upstream `applyEffect()` logic. It runs after initial effect collection and before the final range update. `Apply` effects are the primary target: when the called function has a known signature entry in `fn_signatures`, each argument is mapped per-parameter — `Mutate` argument effect becomes `MutateTransitively`, `Capture` stays `Capture`, `Freeze` stays `Freeze`, and alias-to-return effects produce a new `Alias` between the argument place and the call's return place. When no signature is available the conservative path emits `MutateTransitiveConditionally` for every argument, matching upstream's fallback. A `value_kind()` method was added to `AbstractHeap` to power the remaining refinements: `CreateFrom`/`Assign` from a Primitive or Global collapse to `Create(Primitive)`; from a Frozen source they become `Create(Frozen)` + `ImmutableCapture`. `Capture` of a Primitive or Global is dropped (primitives cannot be aliased); of a Frozen place it becomes `ImmutableCapture`. `MutateConditionally`/`Mutate` of a Frozen place emit `MutateFrozen`. The `aliasing_effects.rs` instruction handler was updated to accept `fn_signatures` and perform signature lookups at `CallExpression`, `NewExpression`, and `TaggedTemplateExpression` sites, passing the resolved `FunctionSignature` (or `None`) into the `Apply` effect that `refine_effects()` later processes. `pipeline.rs` wires the new data flow: `analyse_functions` runs first and its output map is threaded into `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects`. Conformance moved from 370 → 385/1717 (+15 fixtures, 22.4%), 0 panics.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/analyse_functions.rs` | Complete rewrite: produces `FxHashMap<IdentifierId, FunctionSignature>`; per-parameter effect extraction with `StoreLocal`/`LoadLocal`/`TypeCast` alias resolution; fixpoint propagation loop for transitive callee signatures |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` | Added `refine_effects()` implementing `applyEffect()`: signature-aware `Apply` resolution, conservative fallback, `CreateFrom`/`Assign`/`Capture`/`MutateConditionally`/`Mutate` refinement via `value_kind()`; added `value_kind()` to `AbstractHeap`; updated function signature to accept `fn_signatures` map |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/aliasing_effects.rs` | Added `fn_signatures` parameter; signature lookups at `CallExpression`, `NewExpression`, `TaggedTemplateExpression` call sites; resolved `FunctionSignature` passed into `Apply` effect |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Wired `analyse_functions` → `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects` data flow; `fn_signatures` map threaded through pipeline |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 15 newly-passing fixture entries |

---

## Phase 69: `refine_effects()` — Apply Resolution and Value-Kind-Based Effect Refinement

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/over-memoization-bailout.md -- Gap 5
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingEffects.ts` (`applyEffect()`)

Added the `refine_effects()` phase (Phase 3.5 in `infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs`) which implements the upstream `applyEffect()` logic. This pass runs after the initial effect collection and before the final range update. It iterates over all collected effects and resolves or refines them based on the abstract heap's current value-kind knowledge, replacing high-level abstract effects with concrete lower-level ones.

The most structurally significant case is `Apply` resolution. When the called function has a known signature, each argument effect is mapped per-parameter: `Mutate` → `MutateTransitively`, `Capture` → standard `Capture`, `Freeze` → `Freeze`, and alias-to-return effects produce a new `Alias` entry between the argument and return place. When no signature is available, the conservative path emits `MutateTransitiveConditionally` for every argument — matching upstream's fallback. The remaining cases refine effects using a new `value_kind()` method added to `AbstractHeap`: `CreateFrom` on a Primitive or Global place collapses to a plain `Create(Primitive)`; on a Frozen place it becomes `Create(Frozen)` plus an `ImmutableCapture`. `Assign` follows the same pattern — from Primitive/Global it becomes `Create(Primitive)`, from Frozen it becomes `Create(Frozen)` plus `ImmutableCapture`. `Capture` of a Primitive or Global is dropped entirely (primitives cannot be aliased); of a Frozen place it becomes `ImmutableCapture`. `MutateConditionally` and `Mutate` of a Primitive, Global, or Frozen place are either dropped or emit a `MutateFrozen` error, depending on the freeze status. Three code-review fixes were incorporated during the session: the P0 Apply signature-aware resolution (the most impactful correctness change), a P1 fix ensuring `Assign` from a Frozen source emits a `Create(Frozen)` rather than being silently dropped, and a P2 replacement of wildcard match arms with explicit variants for exhaustiveness safety. The pass closed 15 conformance fixtures (370 → 385/1717, 22.4%).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_effects.rs` | Added `refine_effects()` function implementing `applyEffect()` logic: `Apply` resolution with/without signature, `CreateFrom`/`Assign`/`Capture`/`MutateConditionally`/`Mutate` refinement via value-kind analysis; added `value_kind()` method to `AbstractHeap` |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 15 newly-passing fixture entries |

---

## Phase 68: Graph-Based BFS Mutation Propagation in InferMutationAliasingRanges

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/scope-merging.md -- Mutation aliasing ranges rewrite
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutationAliasingRanges.ts`

Rewrote `infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges.rs` from a flat one-level alias traversal (~315 lines) to a graph-based BFS mutation propagation algorithm (~715 lines). The previous implementation used three parallel maps — `alias_map`, `mutation_map`, and `last_use_map` — with a single-step alias resolution that could not propagate mutations transitively through multi-hop alias chains (e.g., A aliases B captures C, mutation of C never reached A). The new implementation builds a directed `AliasingGraph` during the instruction scan phase and then processes all collected mutations via BFS in a deferred second phase.

The central data structure is `AliasingGraph` with `Node` entries that store forward edges plus typed backward sets (`aliases`, `created_from`, `captures`, `maybe_aliases`). Mutations are collected as `PendingMutation` work items and processed by the `mutate()` BFS function, which follows edges with temporal index guards — only edges created before the mutation's instruction index are followed, matching the upstream rule that aliasing created after a mutation cannot retroactively extend the mutable range. Phi-node back-edges are handled via a `pending_phis` map: when BFS reaches a phi node that was added before its predecessor blocks were processed, the phi edge is deferred and replayed after all blocks complete. A `phi_ids` set prevents backward alias traversal through phi nodes encountered via forward edges, preventing infinite cycles. For backward compatibility, `creation_map` and `last_use_map` from the original implementation were retained, with `creation_map` extended to cover `CreateFunction` and `CreateFrom` instructions missed in the previous version. All `unwrap()` calls were eliminated via a unified `add_edge()` helper method that returns `Option` and propagates through `?`. A P0 edge-ordering bug (BFS loop used `break` instead of `continue` for deferred phi edges) was fixed during code review, and a P2 suspicious `range.start` mutation was removed. Conformance held at 370/1717 with zero regressions.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/inference/infer_mutation_aliasing_ranges.rs` | Full rewrite: `AliasingGraph` + `Node` + `PendingMutation` + `WorkItem` data structures; BFS `mutate()` with temporal guards; `pending_phis` map + `phi_ids` set for back-edge handling; `add_edge()` unified helper; `creation_map` extended for `CreateFunction`/`CreateFrom`; all `unwrap()` calls eliminated; P0 `break→continue` fix; P2 `range.start` mutation removed (~315 → ~715 lines) |

---

## Phase 67: Hook Alias Detection and Dynamic Hook Identity Validation

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/validation.md -- Hook alias detection, dynamic hook identity validation
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateHooksUsage.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/HIR/Environment.ts`

Hook alias detection was added end-to-end: a new `collect_hook_aliases()` pass in `program.rs` scans all import declarations in the AST for aliased hook imports (e.g., `import { useFragment as readFragment } from 'relay'`) and populates a new `hook_aliases: FxHashSet<String>` field on `EnvironmentConfig`. The field is threaded through `pipeline.rs` into `validate_hooks_usage`. Inside the validator, all four existing rules (conditional calls, method calls, hooks-as-values, nested function calls) were updated to use a unified `is_hook()` closure that checks both `is_hook_name()` (the standard `use` prefix heuristic) and presence in the alias set. The alias set is also propagated into the recursive `check_hooks_in_nested_functions` and `check_nested_hir_for_hook_calls` helpers so nested scopes get the same alias awareness.

A new Rule 5 — dynamic hook identity validation — was added to detect when a hook-named callee is not a stable reference. The check resolves the callee through `StoreLocal` chains: if the callee name comes from a non-import, non-parameter, non-constant source (e.g., `const useX = someFunc(); useX()`), a `DynamicHookIdentity` diagnostic is emitted. This matches the upstream behavior from `ValidateHooksUsage.ts` where hook callees whose values are not statically determinable are flagged. Five snapshot files were also updated to reflect improved dependency minimization and earlier error detection that became visible once aliases were properly excluded from the reactive dependency graph. Together these changes close 31 conformance fixtures (1332→1301 known failures).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_hooks_usage.rs` | Added `hook_aliases` parameter; unified `is_hook()` closure for alias+name checking; applied to Rules 1, 1b, 3, 4; added Rule 5 dynamic hook identity check via `StoreLocal` chain resolution; propagated aliases into recursive helpers |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Passes `config.hook_aliases` to `validate_hooks_usage` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/program.rs` | Added `collect_hook_aliases()` function that scans import declarations for aliased hook bindings; added `FxHashSet` import |

## Phase 66: Destructuring Assignment Lowering & Global Reassignment Detection

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/upstream-errors.md -- Gap 9 (upstream error fixtures)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/HIR/BuildHIR.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateLocalsNotReassignedAfterRender.ts`

Two independent features were added to close three additional conformance fixtures. The first is proper destructuring assignment lowering in `build.rs`. Previously, assignment expressions whose left-hand side was an `ArrayPattern` or `ObjectPattern` fell through to an `UnsupportedNode("DestructuringAssignment")` stub. The fix iterates each destructuring element: for array patterns, it emits a `ComputedLoad` with an integer-index property then a `StoreLocal` (or `StoreGlobal` if the target identifier is a global name); for object patterns, it emits a `PropertyLoad` keyed by the property name then the corresponding store. This brings the HIR lowering for `[a, b] = value` and `{a, b} = value` inline with what upstream BuildHIR.ts emits for the same patterns.

The second feature extends `validate_no_global_reassignment.rs` with a component-level `StoreLocal` reassignment check. Previously, the validator only detected outer-scope reassignments from inside nested functions; plain `x = ...` at the component body level was invisible unless it was already handled by a different pass. The fix adds a top-level walk over all component-scope instructions: any `StoreLocal` whose lvalue identifier name is not in the component's declared-locals set is flagged as a `GlobalReassignment` diagnostic. This matches what upstream's `validateLocalsNotReassignedAfterRender` does at the function level. Together these changes unlock three fixtures — two destructuring-assignment-to-global tests and one should-bailout infer-mode fixture.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/build.rs` | Added destructuring assignment lowering: `ArrayPattern` lhs emits `ComputedLoad` + `StoreLocal`/`StoreGlobal` per element; `ObjectPattern` lhs emits `PropertyLoad` + `StoreLocal`/`StoreGlobal` per property |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_global_reassignment.rs` | Added component-level `StoreLocal` reassignment check: walks all component-scope instructions and flags any `StoreLocal` whose target name is not in the declared-locals set |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 3 newly-passing fixtures: `error.invalid-destructure-assignment-to-global.js`, `error.invalid-destructure-to-local-global-variables.js`, `should-bailout-without-compilation-infer-mode.js` |

## Phase 65: Hook-Call Capture Freeze Detection

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/upstream-errors.md -- Gap 9 (upstream error fixtures)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutableRanges.ts`

The root cause of four remaining freeze-detection fixtures was that `HIRFunction.context` is always `Vec::new()` for nested arrow/function expressions — the HIR builder never populates captured variable lists for inner functions. The `func_captures` map in `validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` relied on `lowered_func.context` being populated, so captures were never collected for any nested function, making freeze violations inside closures invisible.

The fix replaces the context-based approach with a body-scan approach: a new `collect_inner_declared_names` helper walks all blocks of an inner function's HIR body and collects every identifier bound by `StoreLocal`, `StoreContext`, `Declare`, or function-parameter declarations. During the capture-collection pass, any `LoadLocal` or `LoadContext` instruction that references a name not in this inner-declared set is treated as a capture of the outer scope. This correctly handles the cases where a hook-call result (e.g., the return value of `useState`) is frozen by the outer component and then mutated inside a nested function that captures it.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` | Replaced `context`-based capture collection with body-scan approach; added `collect_inner_declared_names` helper that walks all HIR blocks for locally declared names; capture detection now uses `LoadLocal`/`LoadContext` references not in the declared set |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 4 newly-passing fixtures: `error.assign-ref-in-effect-hint.js`, `error.hook-call-freezes-captured-identifier.tsx`, `error.hook-call-freezes-captured-memberexpr.jsx`, `error.invalid-hook-function-argument-mutates-local-variable.js` |

## Phase 64: Gap 9 Mutation Tracking Validation Errors — Delete Lowering, Phi Freeze Propagation, Alias Freeze, Derivation Chains, and Outer-Scope Property Mutation

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/upstream-errors.md -- Gap 9 (upstream error fixtures)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutableRanges.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateLocalsNotReassignedAfterRender.ts`

Six distinct sub-features were added to `validate_no_mutation_after_freeze` and `validate_no_global_reassignment` to close ten upstream error fixtures. First, delete expression lowering in `build.rs` was fixed: `delete x.y` and `delete x[i]` previously emitted `UnaryExpression { op: Delete }` and were invisible to mutation detection; they now emit `PropertyDelete`/`ComputedDelete` HIR nodes, enabling frozen-value mutation detection for delete operations. Second, phi-node freeze propagation was added: when any phi operand is present in `frozen_values`, the phi output is also inserted — this handles cases where `x` flows into a phi and the phi result is later mutated. Third, alias freeze tracking was implemented via an `alias_map: FxHashMap<String, String>` that records `let y = x` LoadLocal assignments; when `x` is frozen, all aliases that map to it are also frozen, with recursive propagation. Fourth, pre-freeze alias propagation was added: aliases of pre-frozen params/hook-returns are frozen at initialization time, not only when the freeze instruction is encountered later.

Fifth, derivation chain tracking was added to detect patterns like `for (const x of props.items) { x.modified = true }` — where `x` is derived from frozen `props` via a `PropertyLoad → GetIterator → IteratorNext → StoreLocal → LoadLocal` chain. The implementation maintains a `derived_from_frozen: FxHashMap<String, String>` map that bridges SSA ID gaps using name-based lookup (a DIVERGENCE from upstream's stable-ID graph traversal). Sixth, outer-scope mutation detection in `validate_no_global_reassignment` was extended: nested functions now check for `PropertyStore` and `MethodCall` operations on undeclared outer-scope variables (not just `StoreLocal` reassignment). Additionally, render helper detection was extended to check `PropertyStore` and `MethodCall` on globals — nested functions returning JSX are scanned for these operations.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/hir/build.rs` | Added delete expression special-casing: `delete x.y` emits `PropertyDelete`, `delete x[i]` emits `ComputedDelete` instead of `UnaryExpression { op: Delete }` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` | Added phi-node freeze propagation, alias freeze tracking via `alias_map`, derivation chain tracking via `derived_from_frozen`, pre-freeze alias propagation, and hook-return recheck for alias-chained values |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_global_reassignment.rs` | Extended outer-scope mutation to detect `PropertyStore`/`MethodCall` on undeclared outer-scope variables; added `PropertyStore`/`MethodCall` checks to render helper global mutation detection |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 10 newly-passing fixtures (delete, phi-freeze, alias-freeze, derivation chain, outer-scope property mutation, render helper) |

## Phase 63: Known-Incompatible Module Detection, ESLint Suppression Bail-Out, useMemo Deps Validation, and Capitalized Call Alias Resolution

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/upstream-errors.md -- Gap 9 (upstream error fixtures)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Entrypoint/Program.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateUseMemo.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateNoCapitalizedCalls.ts`

Four validation/bail-out features were added to close six upstream error fixtures from Gap 9. The first two are file-level bail-outs implemented in `program.rs`. `has_known_incompatible_import` scans all import declarations before compilation begins and returns an error if any source value is `ReactCompilerKnownIncompatibleTest`; upstream emits a per-component diagnostic, but our implementation bails the entire file — a DIVERGENCE. `has_eslint_hooks_suppression` performs a raw string scan over the source text looking for unclosed `eslint-disable` comments targeting `react-hooks/rules-of-hooks` or `react-hooks/exhaustive-deps`; if found, compilation is skipped for the entire file — again a DIVERGENCE from upstream's per-component diagnostic. The raw-string approach avoids parsing comment nodes and is sufficient for the fixture pattern.

The third feature extends `validate_use_memo.rs` with a `check_deps_is_array_literal` sub-check that rejects non-array-literal dependency lists in `useMemo` and `useCallback` calls. It walks the HIR to find the defining instruction of the deps argument and verifies it is either an `ArrayExpression` or a `Primitive::Undefined` (the "no deps" case); any other instruction kind — including conditional expressions — produces an error. The fourth feature fixes `validate_no_capitalized_calls.rs`'s `id_to_name` alias resolution to propagate through `StoreLocal` and `StoreContext` instruction chains, so that patterns like `let x = Bar; x()` correctly detect the capitalized name `Bar` rather than the alias `x`. These four features together unlock six fixtures that were previously in `known-failures.txt`, raising conformance from 368 to 374/1717.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/program.rs` | Added `has_known_incompatible_import` (pre-compilation import scan) and `has_eslint_hooks_suppression` (raw source string scan for unclosed eslint-disable directives) |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_use_memo.rs` | Added `check_deps_is_array_literal` sub-check: walks HIR to verify deps argument defining instruction is `ArrayExpression` or `Primitive::Undefined` |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_capitalized_calls.rs` | Extended `id_to_name` propagation through `StoreLocal`/`StoreContext` chains to resolve capitalized name aliases |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 6 newly-passing fixtures |

## Phase 62: DeclarationId-Based Dependency Identity in propagate_dependencies and merge_scopes

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/memoization-structure.md -- Sub-task 4f (DeclarationId-based dep matching)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependencies.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/MergeReactiveScopesThatInvalidateTogether.ts`

Dependency comparison and deduplication throughout the scope-merging pipeline was previously string-based — identifiers were matched by name. This is structurally incorrect because two distinct variables can share a name (e.g. shadowing in nested scopes), and a single variable can be accessed under multiple names after SSA renaming. Upstream uses `DeclarationId` (a stable integer identity assigned at HIR construction) to distinguish bindings.

In `propagate_dependencies.rs`, `TemporaryInfo` gains a `root_declaration_id: Option<DeclarationId>` field that carries the stable binding identity alongside the existing name. The `scope_written_names: FxHashSet<String>` map is replaced with `scope_written_decl_ids: FxHashSet<DeclarationId>`, and `name_consumers` and `decl_deps_map` switch their string keys to `DeclarationId` keys. Dep deduplication and sort ordering now compare `(DeclarationId, path)` pairs rather than `(name, path)` pairs. In `merge_scopes.rs`, `DepKey` is changed from `(Option<String>, Vec<DependencyPathEntry>)` to `(Option<DeclarationId>, IdentifierId, Vec<DependencyPathEntry>)` — the `IdentifierId` is kept alongside `DeclarationId` because the display name reconstruction (used in codegen) still requires it. The `dep_key_set` in `can_merge_scopes`, `merge_scope_deps`, and `flatten_nested_identical_scopes` all use the new key type. All `TODO(4f)` annotations and the now-obsolete DIVERGENCE comments about name-based matching are removed. Conformance is unchanged at 368/1717 — this is a correctness improvement and structural prerequisite for future scope-merging gains rather than a feature addition.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | Added `root_declaration_id` to `TemporaryInfo`; replaced `scope_written_names`, `name_consumers`, and `decl_deps_map` string keys with `DeclarationId` keys; updated deduplication and sort |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/merge_scopes.rs` | Changed `DepKey` to `(Option<DeclarationId>, IdentifierId, Vec<DependencyPathEntry>)`; updated `dep_key_set` in `can_merge_scopes`, `merge_scope_deps`, and `flatten_nested_identical_scopes`; removed TODO(4f) and obsolete DIVERGENCE comments |

---

## Phase 61: Pre-freeze Component Props and Hook Arguments in validate_no_mutation_after_freeze

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/upstream-errors.md -- Gap 1 (Frozen Mutation Detection)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateLocalsNotReassignedAfterRender.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Inference/InferMutableRanges.ts`

`validate_no_mutation_after_freeze` was only freezing values at the point of explicit freeze instructions encountered during the block walk, meaning component props and hook arguments were not treated as frozen from the start of execution. Upstream handles this by propagating `frozen` state transitively through `InferMutableRanges` during the inference phase; since our port does not have a full `InferMutableRanges` equivalent, the approximation is to pre-freeze all function parameters (component props and hook arguments) at the start of the validation pass — this is a DIVERGENCE from upstream.

The implementation adds a `param_names: &[String]` parameter to `validate_no_mutation_after_freeze`, which is already extracted from `HIRFunction.params` in the pipeline and was already being passed to other validation functions. The pre-freeze loop inserts all param names into the `frozen_values` set before any block walk begins. An earlier iteration of the fix scanned the entry block for `DeclareLocal` instructions to infer param-like locals, but this over-froze ordinary local variables, producing 27 spurious additional matches. The corrected approach uses the explicit `param_names` slice, which contributed exactly 6 genuine new matches. The 6 newly passing fixtures all involve patterns where a component receives props, the props object (or a destructured value from it) is passed into a helper or stored, and that helper later mutates the value — cases that require knowing the props are frozen from function entry.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_mutation_after_freeze.rs` | Added `param_names: &[String]` parameter; pre-freeze loop inserts all param names into `frozen_values` before block walk |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Updated call site to pass `param_names` slice to `validate_no_mutation_after_freeze` |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 6 newly-passing fixtures |

## Phase 60: Nested Function Scanning in validate_no_ref_access_in_render and Transitive setState Detection in validate_no_set_state_in_render

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/upstream-errors.md -- Gap 5 (ref access in nested functions), Gap 7 (setState in nested functions)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateNoRefAccessInRender.ts`, `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/Validation/ValidateNoSetStateInRender.ts`

`validate_no_ref_access_in_render` was only scanning top-level component instructions, missing ref accesses inside nested function bodies (callbacks passed to `useReducer`, `useState` initializers, and functions invoked during render). The fix adds a recursive nested-function scanning phase: after the main instruction walk, any `FunctionExpression` or `ObjectMethod` value encountered is recursively walked for `PropertyLoad` and `PropertyStore` instructions whose object name is present in the accumulated `ref_names` set. Ref alias detection is also added — when a `StoreLocal` stores a value whose source name is in `ref_names`, the destination name is also added to `ref_names`, allowing patterns like `const aliasedRef = ref; aliasedRef.current` to be caught. Ref tracking uses an `FxHashSet<String>` with name-based identity, which is a DIVERGENCE from upstream's stable-identifier approach but is consistent with the name-based tracking used throughout the other validation passes.

`validate_no_set_state_in_render` was only detecting direct `setState` calls at the top-level component scope, missing cases where a nested `FunctionExpression` calls `setState` and that function is then called during render. The fix introduces a two-phase analysis. First, all `FunctionExpression` lvalues are mapped to their defining temp identifiers, and for each nested function body a scan checks whether any instruction performs a `LoadContext` of a known `setState` variable followed by a call, or makes a direct `CallExpression` to a `setState`-named callee. Functions identified as "calling setState" are recorded by their temp identifier. Second, a fixpoint loop propagates transitivity: if a function `foo` calls function `bar`, and `bar` eventually calls `setState`, then `foo` is also marked as calling setState. The loop iterates until no new functions are added. Finally, during the main component instruction walk, any `CallExpression` whose callee resolves to a temp that is in the "calls setState" set is flagged as an error. Lvalue-to-name resolution threads through `StoreLocal` chains because `FunctionExpression` lvalues are unnamed temporaries. Eight fixtures that were previously in `known-failures.txt` now pass, raising conformance from 354 to 362/1717 (+8, 21.1%).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_ref_access_in_render.rs` | Added recursive nested function scanning, ref alias detection via `StoreLocal` tracking, `FxHashSet<String>` ref name propagation across scope boundaries |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/validation/validate_no_set_state_in_render.rs` | Added transitive setState detection: function-to-temp mapping, per-function setState scan, fixpoint chain resolution loop, temp-to-name propagation through `StoreLocal` |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 8 newly-passing fixtures |

---

## Phase 59: Free Variable Detection and Hook Call Exclusion in propagate_scope_dependencies_hir

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/memoization-structure.md -- Gap 6 (over-scoped deps), Gap 3 (slot count alignment)
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependenciesHIR.ts`

`propagate_scope_dependencies_hir` was treating every `LoadLocal`/`LoadContext` operand as a potential reactive dependency, including identifiers that refer to imported components, module-scope values, and other free variables (e.g. `Foo` in `<Foo />`, `MaybeMutable` in `new MaybeMutable()`). Upstream avoids this problem because its `BuildHIR` pass uses a scope chain that marks free variables during HIR construction; our port does not have that scope chain, so the distinction had to be reconstructed here. The fix adds a two-phase first pass: collect `locally_defined_names` from `StoreLocal`, `DeclareLocal`, and `Destructure` lvalues plus function parameter names (passed in via a new `param_names` argument to `run_pipeline`); then, during the main dependency-collection walk, any `LoadLocal`/`LoadContext` whose identifier name is not in `locally_defined_names` and not already in `non_reactive_names` is classified as a free variable and added to `non_reactive_names` — preventing it from ever becoming a scope dependency. An `id_to_name` map is also built during the first pass to enable name lookups in the second pass. A `collect_destructure_names` helper recursively extracts all binding names from `DestructurePattern` nodes.

A second bug was discovered in the pre-existing `CallExpression` non-reactivity rule: it was marking the *result* of any call as non-reactive, including hook calls like `useState(0)` and `useRef(null)`. This caused hook return values to be stripped from scope dependencies, breaking memoization for components that read from hook returns. The fix adds a hook-exclusion guard: if the callee's name begins with `"use"` followed by an uppercase letter (matching React's hook naming convention), the non-reactivity rule is skipped. This is a DIVERGENCE from upstream, which handles this distinction structurally via its scope chain and HIR construction rather than with a name-based guard. Five fixtures that were failing due to these spurious free-variable dependencies now pass, raising conformance from 349 to 354/1717 (+5, 20.6%).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | Added `locally_defined_names` collection, `id_to_name` map, free variable detection in first pass, hook exclusion guard in `CallExpression` non-reactivity rule, `collect_destructure_names` helper |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/entrypoint/pipeline.rs` | Added `param_names` parameter to `run_pipeline`, `extract_param_names` helper to collect function parameter binding names |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/tests/pass_unit_tests.rs` | Updated call site to pass `param_names` argument |
| `tests/conformance/known-failures.txt` | Removed 5 newly-passing fixtures |

## Phase 58: Fix Sentinel Scope Slot Count Off-By-One in codegen.rs

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/memoization-structure.md -- Gap 3
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/CodegenReactApp/CodegenReactFunction.ts`

Sentinel scopes were allocated `1 + N` cache slots (one sentinel slot plus one per declaration), but upstream `CodegenReactFunction.ts` allocates exactly `N` slots for sentinel scopes — the sentinel check reuses the first declaration's slot index rather than claiming a dedicated slot. The off-by-one caused the emitted `_c` array to be one element too large for every component containing a sentinel scope, and all subsequent slot indices were shifted by one relative to what the fixtures expect.

The fix touches three locations in `codegen.rs`: `count_cache_slots` now counts sentinel scopes as `declarations.len()` instead of `1 + declarations.len()`; `codegen_scope` allocates the slot index for sentinel scopes at `declarations[0]`'s offset rather than a fresh leading slot; and the slot allocation loop no longer skips the first declaration. Four snapshot files were regenerated to reflect the corrected slot layout. Seven fixtures that were previously producing wrong `_c` sizes now emit correct output and were removed from `known-failures.txt`, raising conformance from 342 to 349/1717 (+7).

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/codegen/codegen.rs` | `count_cache_slots` sentinel branch uses `declarations.len()`; `codegen_scope` slot allocation corrected; leading-slot skip removed |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__basic_memoization.snap` | Updated slot indices |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__hook_dependencies.snap` | Updated slot indices |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__multiple_scopes.snap` | Updated slot indices |
| `tests/snapshots/snapshot_tests__component_with_derived_value.snap` | Updated slot indices |
| `tests/fixtures/known-failures.txt` | Removed 7 newly-passing fixtures: `infer-functions-component-with-jsx.js`, `infer-functions-hook-with-jsx.js`, `jsx-html-entity.js`, `jsx-preserve-escape-character.js`, `repro-duplicate-type-import.tsx`, `target-flag-meta-internal.js`, `target-flag.js` |

## Phase 57: Fix LoadGlobal — Global Binding Names Added to non_reactive_names

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/memoization-structure.md -- Gap 6
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependenciesHIR.ts`

`propagate_dependencies` maintains a `non_reactive_names` set to track identifiers that should not be promoted to reactive scope dependencies. Previously, `LoadGlobal` instructions were not adding the loaded binding's name to this set. As a result, when a later name-based fallback pass in `propagate_scope_dependencies_hir` iterated over instructions looking for dependency candidates, global names (e.g. `console`, `Math`, `document`) could slip through the filter and be recorded as scope dependencies — causing spurious entries in the dep list and potentially incorrect memoization boundaries.

The fix is a one-line addition in the `LoadGlobal` match arm: the binding's `.name` string is inserted into `non_reactive_names` immediately when the instruction is encountered. This mirrors upstream's handling in `PropagateScopeDependenciesHIR.ts`, where global bindings are excluded from reactive dependency consideration by definition. No new fixtures pass as a result — conformance remains at 342/1717 — but the change closes a structural correctness gap that would otherwise produce incorrect dep sets once other Gap 6 memoization improvements land.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | `LoadGlobal` arm now inserts `binding.name` into `non_reactive_names` |

## Phase 56: Fix prune_non_escaping_scopes — Derived Computations Inside Scope Guards

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/memoization-structure.md -- Gap 11
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PruneNonEscapingScopes.ts`

`prune_non_escaping_scopes` contained a latent bug: the `collect_used_outside_scopes` helper accepted an `in_scope: bool` flag that was set to `true` whenever the traversal entered any `ReactiveScopeBlock`. A variable declared in scope S1 and used inside scope S2 (a different scope) would be seen with `in_scope = true`, causing the helper to skip recording it as "used outside its declaring scope". As a result, S1 appeared non-escaping and was pruned — its instructions were emitted as bare statements outside any cache guard. The `basic_memoization` fixture exposed this directly: `doubled = value * 2` appeared as a plain assignment outside the memoization block instead of being guarded by a scope that checks whether `value` changed.

The fix removes the `in_scope` parameter entirely and renames the function to `collect_used_ids`. The new implementation collects every operand `Place` ID unconditionally, regardless of scope nesting depth, then the caller computes "escaping" as the set difference between these uses and the scope's own declared IDs. This matches upstream `PruneNonEscapingScopes.ts`, which also collects all usages without any scope-membership guard. The change is purely in how uses are gathered; the escape predicate logic and the prune/emit decision are unchanged. Five snapshot files were updated to reflect that derived values (`doubled`, `greeting`, property loads cached in temporaries) are now correctly emitted inside their respective scope guards with a proper cache slot check.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/prune_scopes.rs` | Removed `in_scope` flag from `collect_used_outside_scopes`; renamed to `collect_used_ids`; unconditional operand collection |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__basic_memoization.snap` | `doubled` now emitted inside scope guard |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__hook_dependencies.snap` | Derived deps emitted inside scope guards |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__multiple_scopes.snap` | Multiple scope guards correctly structured |
| `tests/snapshots/snapshot_tests__component_with_derived_value.snap` | Updated codegen snapshot |
| `tests/snapshots/fixture_tests__component-with-derived_tsx.snap` | Updated fixture snapshot |

## Phase 55: Transitive Dependency Resolution and StoreLocal Declaration Tracking

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/memoization-structure.md -- Gap 3: Dependency propagation
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/PropagateScopeDependenciesHIR.ts`

Two coordinated changes to `propagate_scope_dependencies_hir` address the root cause of identical-dep-set merge failures. The first (Phase 3 enhancement) fixes StoreLocal/StoreContext target tracking: when a Store instruction's target identifier is used outside the declaring scope, it is now registered as a scope declaration. A name-based consumer matching strategy bridges SSA ID mismatches — our HIR generates fresh `Place` IDs per occurrence, so declaration and use sites carry different numeric IDs; matching by `identifier.name` resolves this. This mirrors upstream's `collectTemporariesSidemap` / `visitOperand` pattern where SSA temporaries are resolved back to their root reactive inputs. The second change (Phase 3.5) introduces a fixpoint loop that builds a `decl_deps_map` mapping declared variable names to their declaring scope's dependency set, then substitutes transitive dependencies: when scope B lists `doubled` (itself declared by scope A with dep `[value]`) as a dependency, the loop replaces that dep entry with `[value]`. The fixpoint iterates until no substitution changes occur, collapsing arbitrarily deep dependency chains.

Verified on the `basic_memoization` fixture: both scopes for the `Doubler` component now resolve to `[value]` as their shared dep set, matching upstream behavior exactly, which is the prerequisite for the `can_merge_scopes` identical-dep-set branch to fire. Conformance is unchanged at 342/1717 — transitive resolution is structural; downstream codegen fidelity gaps (e.g. codegen slot layout, output variable naming) prevent new fixture matches independently. A known limitation is that name-based matching (noted as TODO(4f) in the code) can false-positive on shadowed variables in the same scope, the same trade-off already accepted by `scope_written_names` and `dep_key_set` elsewhere in the codebase.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/propagate_dependencies.rs` | StoreLocal/StoreContext targets tracked as scope declarations via name-based consumer matching; fixpoint transitive dep substitution loop (`decl_deps_map`) |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__basic_memoization.snap` | Updated to reflect revised dep propagation output |
| `tests/snapshots/snapshot_tests__basic_memoization.snap` | Updated snapshot |
| `tests/snapshots/fixture_tests__basic_memoization.snap` | Updated snapshot |
| `tests/snapshots/codegen_validation_tests__basic_memoization.snap` | Updated snapshot |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__hook_dependencies.snap` | Updated snapshot |
| `tests/snapshots/snapshot_tests__hook_dependencies.snap` | Updated snapshot |

## Phase 54: MergeReactiveScopesThatInvalidateTogether — Nested Scope Flattening

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/memoization-structure.md -- Sub-task 4c: Nested scope flattening
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/MergeReactiveScopesThatInvalidateTogether.ts`

Implemented `flatten_nested_identical_scopes(block: &mut ReactiveBlock)` in `merge_scopes.rs`, corresponding to the nested-flattening portion of upstream's `MergeReactiveScopesThatInvalidateTogether`. The algorithm scans each instruction in a `ReactiveBlock` looking for a `ReactiveScopeBlock` that contains exactly one child instruction which is itself a `ReactiveScopeBlock`. When found, it compares the two scopes' dependency sets using `DepKey` set equality (the same key abstraction already used by Phase 53's `can_merge_scopes`). If the sets are identical, the inner scope is flattened into the outer: the outer scope absorbs the inner's `declarations`, `merged` list, and instruction block, then the inner scope wrapper is discarded entirely. The function runs in a `loop { changed = false; ... if !changed { break; } }` pattern so that multi-level nesting (outer ⊇ middle ⊇ inner, all identical deps) is collapsed in successive passes without requiring manual recursion.

The function is inserted as "Pass 1.5" inside `merge_scopes_in_block`, after the Pass 1 recursive descent into child terminals (which must complete first so inner structures are already settled) and before the Pass 2 merge-plan walk that reasons about adjacent scope candidates. This placement mirrors upstream's ordering. All 158 tests continue to pass; `cargo check` and `clippy` are clean. Conformance is unchanged at 342/1717 — this pass does not independently unlock new fixtures but is a required structural prerequisite for the compound gains expected from the full 4b+4c+4f integration.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/merge_scopes.rs` | Added `flatten_nested_identical_scopes`; wired as Pass 1.5 in `merge_scopes_in_block` |

## Phase 53: MergeReactiveScopesThatInvalidateTogether — Output-to-Input Chaining and Full Merge Loop

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/memoization-structure.md -- Sub-task 4b: Output-to-input scope chaining in invalidate-together merge
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/MergeReactiveScopesThatInvalidateTogether.ts`

Rewrote `merge_scopes_in_block` with a 3-pass algorithm matching upstream's `MergeReactiveScopesThatInvalidateTogether.ts`. Pass 1 recurses into nested terminal blocks first — ordering matters because inner-scope merges must be settled before the outer walk can reason about gap instructions. Pass 2 walks all instructions using a `MergeCandidate` state machine: when a scope block is encountered, it either becomes the initial candidate or is tested for mergeability against the current candidate; plain instructions between scope blocks are accumulated via the existing `accumulate_intermediate_instruction` / `IntermediateAccumulator` infrastructure from Phase 51. Pass 3 reconstructs `block.instructions` by absorbing gap instructions and absorbee scope declarations/reassignments into each winner scope, then emitting the merged scope block in place of the original.

Two new helpers drive the merge decision. `can_merge_scopes(prev, next, intermediates, last_usage_map) -> bool` checks two independent conditions: (1) identical dependency sets — same dependency keys in the same order — meaning the scopes always invalidate together by definition, or (2) output-to-input chaining — every dependency of `next` either matches an always-invalidating declaration of `prev` (i.e., `prev` produces what `next` consumes) and the intermediate gap instructions are safe (verified via `are_lvalues_last_used_by_scope`). `merge_scope_deps` deduplicates the combined dependency list when two scopes are merged, preserving the first occurrence of each unique dep key. All four Phase 4d infrastructure functions (`accumulate_intermediate_instruction`, `are_lvalues_last_used_by_scope`, `scope_is_eligible_for_merging`, `build_last_usage_map`) are now actively called, so all `#[expect(dead_code)]` annotations were removed. A stale underscore omission in `build_last_usage_map` (introduced by an earlier edit) was also corrected. One snapshot was updated (`per_pass_snapshots__hook_dependencies`). Conformance is unchanged at 342/1717 — compound gains from this pass are expected to materialize together with Sub-tasks 4c and 4f once the full pipeline is integrated.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/merge_scopes.rs` | Rewrote `merge_scopes_in_block` with 3-pass algorithm; added `can_merge_scopes` and `merge_scope_deps` helpers; removed all `#[expect(dead_code)]` annotations; fixed `build_last_usage_map` function name |
| `tests/snapshots/per_pass_snapshots__hook_dependencies.snap` | Updated snapshot reflecting revised scope merge output |

---

## Phase 52: MergeReactiveScopesThatInvalidateTogether — `scope_is_eligible_for_merging` Predicate

**Date:** 2026-03-14
**Task:** .todo/memoization-structure.md -- Sub-task 4e: `scopeIsEligibleForMerging` predicate
**Upstream:** `compiler/packages/babel-plugin-react-compiler/src/ReactiveScopes/MergeReactiveScopesThatInvalidateTogether.ts`

Added `scope_is_eligible_for_merging(scope_block: &ReactiveScopeBlock) -> bool` to `merge_scopes.rs`. This is a pure predicate that mirrors upstream's `scopeIsEligibleForMerging` function exactly: a scope is eligible for merging only if (1) it has no reassignments (empty `reassignments` set on the `ReactiveScope`) and (2) at least one of its declared identifiers has an always-invalidating type — specifically `Object` or `Function` in the `Type` enum. Both conditions must hold simultaneously; any reassignment disqualifies the scope regardless of declaration types.

The predicate operates by checking `scope.scope.reassignments.is_empty()` first, then iterating `scope.scope.declarations` and calling `is_always_invalidating_type` on each declaration's `identifier.type_`. The `is_always_invalidating_type` helper (already present from the Phase 4d infrastructure) returns `true` for `Type::Object` and `Type::Function`. This is a purely additive change — the predicate is defined but the call site that integrates it into the merge decision loop (Sub-task 4b) is not yet wired, so there is no behavioral change and conformance is unchanged (342/1717). With 4a (overlap detection), 4d (safety-check infrastructure), and 4e (eligibility predicate) all complete, Sub-task 4b — the actual merge loop — is now fully unblocked.

### Modified files:

| File | Change |
| ---- | ------ |
| `crates/oxc_react_compiler/src/reactive_scopes/merge_scopes.rs` | Added `scope_is_eligible_for_merging` predicate checking no-reassignments + always-invalidating-type declaration |
